29b6(phal chen): dang ldan pa'i chos smra bar gyur cig/ sems can thams cad chos kyi mdzod rnam par phye ba'i ye shes dang ldan zhing dbye ba med pa dang / gnas pa med pa'i chos la gnas pa rab tu thob pa'i chos smra bar gyur cig/ sems can thad
29b7(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pas shin tu bstad pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i ye shes dang ldan zhing bye ba med pa dang / gnas pa med pa'i chos la gnas pa rab tu thob pa'i chos smra bar gyur cig/ sems cad thams cad yon tan dang bsngag
29b8(phal chen): pa mu med cing zad mi shes pa dang ldan te/ chos thams cad khong du chud pa'i chos smra bar gyur cig/ sems can thams cad bden pa'i mtha'i tshul gyis rjes su zhugs pas 'gro ba thams cad la mi sla ba'i chos smra bar
30a1(phal chen): gyur cig/ sems can thams cad bdud kyi las thams cad khong du chud pa'i ye shes dang ldan zhing bdud thams cad rnam par 'thor ba'i chos smra bar gyur cig/ sems can thams cad bdag gi med pa
30a2(phal chen): dang / yongs su 'dzin pa med pa'i sems dang ldan zhing sangs rgyas thams cad kyis yongs su bzung ba'i chos smra bar gyur cig/ sems can thams cad byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyi stobs kyis smon lam rab tu thob cing / 'gro
30a3(phal chen): ba thams cad bde bar byed pa'i chos smra bar gyur cig/ de yang 'di ltar yongasu sngo ste/ nyams pa med pa'i las kyis yong su sngo'o// nyams pa med pa'i rnam par smin pas yongasu sngo'o// nyams pa med pa'i sems kyis yongasu sdol/ 
30a4(phal chen): nyams pa med pa'i chos la yong su sngo'o// nyams pa med pa'i dngos po la yongs su sngo'o// nyabs pa med pa'i rgyu rnams kyis yongasu sngo'o/ da nyams pa med pa'i chos kyi lam gyis yongasu sngo'o// nyams
30a5(phal chen): ba med pa'i ming mang po dang / tshig mang po dang / yi ge mang por phyir yong su sngo'o// nyams pa med pa'i yongasu sngo ba'i phyir yong su myur nyabs pa med pa'i sems can gyi dod bya ba'i phyir yongs su sngo sde/ 
30a6(phal chen): de ltar byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yongs sngo yang gzugs kyi tshul la chags shing yongasu bsngo'o// 'dod pa la gnas pa'i sgra dong du yongasu mi sngo'o// dri phyir yongasu mi ste'o// ro'i phyir yongasu mi sngo'o// 
30a7(phal chen): reg pa'i phyir yongasu mi sngo'o// 'dod pa la gnas pa'i chos rnams kyi phyir yang yongasu mi sngo'o// mtho ris su skye ba'i phyir yang yongasu mi bsngo'o// 'dod pa spyad pa'i phyir yang yongasu mi sde'o// 'dod pa'i yul la chags/ 
30a8(phal chen): pas kyang yong su mi sngo'o// g.yog 'khor gyi phyir yongasu mi sde'o// dbang phyug don du gnyer bas yongasu mi sngo'o// 'khor ba'i dga' ba'i don du yongasu mi sde'o// 'chi 'pho dang skye ba la gnas shing yongasu mi sngon
30b1(phal chen): dngos po la mngon par mos shing yongs su mi sdor// 'dod pa dang ldan par bya ba'i bsam pas yongs su mi sngo'o// kun gzhil mos pas yongs su mi sngo'o// bsnyen pa'i sems kyis yongs su mi sngo'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba gzhig
30b2(phal chen): pa'i don du yongasu mi sde'o// khams gsum pa la gnas pas kyang yongasu mi sngo'o// bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms par 'jug pa'i ro la chags pas kyang yong su mi sngo'o// nyan thos dang
30b3(phal chen): rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la gnas shing yang yongs su mi sngo'o// 'di ltar 'gro ba thams cad yong su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba'i don du thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir yongasu sde'o// chags
30b4(phal chen): ba med pa'i ye shes la 'jug pa'i phyir yong su sngo'o// bsgrings pa ni/ rang pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir yongasu sngo'o// 'gro ba thams thang 'khor ba nas rab tu gdon pa'i ye shes chen po khong
30b5(phal chen): du chung bar bya ba'i phyir yongasu sngo'o// byang chub tu sems bsrud pa rdo rje lta bu dang / bsam pa brtan pa yong su rdzogs par bya ba'i/ phyir yongasu sngo'o// yun tu 'chi ba med pa'i chos bsgrub pa'i phyir
30b6(phal chen): yongasu bsngo'o// sangs rgyas kyi rigs kyis brgyan pa'i rgyan du ma dang thams cad mkhyen pa'i spyod pas rnam par 'phrul pa yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir yong su sngo'o// chos snang ba thams cad kyi ye shes kyi rdzu 'phrul gyis
30b7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul pa grub par bya ba'i phyir yong su sngo'o// chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa rnam kha'i mthas gtugs pa'i zhing thams cad du byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po la gzhi yong su rdzogs pa
30b8(phal chen): rdob cing phyir mi ldog pa dang / rdo rje lta bu'i go tsho ngon yod pas sems can thams cad kun tu bzang po'i sa la rab tu dgod pa la gnas shing yongasu sngo'o// phye ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par sems can thams
31a1(phal chen): cad rab tu dgrol bar bya ba rgyun mi 'chad pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi sa bsgrings pa med pa thams cad 'jig rten du yang dag par bstan pa'i spyod pa rgyud mi 'chang ba la rab tu gnas par bya ba'i
31a2(phal chen): phyir/ nye bar gnas shing yongasu sngo'o// de de ltar yongasu sngo yang rang bzhin dang mnyam pa'i sems kyis yongasu sngo'o// chos nyid dang mnyam pa'i sems kyis yong su sngo'o// 'gro ba tshad med pa thams cad dang ma
31a3(phal chen): pa'i sems kyis yongasu sngo'o// nyon mongs pa med pa dang mnyam pa'i sems kyis yong su sngo'o// byed pa med pa'i rang bzhin dang mnyam pa'i sems kyis yongs su bsngo'o// chos 'khrugs pa med pa yongasu shes
31a4(phal chen): pa'i sems kyis yong su bsngo'o// dus gsum mnyam dpa nyid du zhugs pa'i sems kyis yong su sngo'o// 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang nga lhar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba'i
31a5(phal chen): sems kyi yongasu sngo'o// mngon par shes pa mnyams bathob pa'i sems kyis yongasu sngo'o// thams cad mkhyen pa'i sgo bal grub pa'i sems kyis yongasu sbyor/ sems can dzang
31a6(phal chen): sems can dmyal ba nas phyir bzlog pa'i phyir yongasu sngo'o// sems can thams cad byol song gi skye gnas su mi dgod pa'i phyir yongasu sngo'o// sems can thams cad gshin rje'i 'jig rten na gnas
31a7(phal chen): pa dgag pa'i phyir yong su sngo'o// sems can thams cad kyi sgrib pa'i chos thams cad spang ba'i phyir yongasu sngo'o// 'gro ba thams cad kyi sems dge ba'i rtsa bas shin tu tshim par bya ba'i phyir yongs su
31a8(phal chen): sde'o// chos kyi 'khor lo dus la bab par bskor bas dga' bar bya ba'i phyir yongasu sde'o// stobs bcu 'khor lo la sems can thams cad gzud pa'i phyir yongasu sde'o// byang chub sems dpa'i'
31b1(phal chen): chos dang / smon lam mtha' dang dbung med pa thob par bya ba 'am/ rnam par dag pa'i chos can du bya ba'i phyir yong su sngo'o// byang chub kyi sems cad shes bsgom pa yongs su rdzogs par bya bas dge ba'i bshes
31b2(phal chen): gnyen grangs med pa thams cad dga' bar bya ba'i sems kyis yong su sngo'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos zab mo la gnas par bya ba'i lhag pa'i bsam pas sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yang dag par gzung zhing / 
31b3(phal chen): ye shes kyi snang ba shin tu 'phags par bya ba'i phyir yongasu sngo'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bsgribs pa med par mngon sum du 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir yongasu sngo'o// sangs rgyas thams cad mngon
31b4(phal chen): du lta bar mngon par mos pas yong su sngo'o// chos snang ba thams cad la mngon par mos pas yong su sngo'o// dog pa med pa'i byang chub sems kyis 'jigs pa med pa la
31b5(phal chen): mngon par mos pas yongasu sngo'o// byang chub sems dpa'i gnas bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i ye shes la mngon par mos pas yongasu sngo'o// sems can thams cad
31b6(phal chen): snying rje chen po rnam par dag pas yongasu bskyab pa la mngon par mos pas yong su sngo'o// sangs rgyas kyi zhing mtha' dag ma lus pa lhag ma med pa thams cad rnam par dag par bya ba dang
31b7(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i rgyan sna tshogs kyis thams cad brgyan par mngon par mos pas yongasu sde'o// bdud kyi las dang bdud kyi zhags pa dang bdud kyi dkrugs ma thams cad rnam par gtor ba dang / rab tu gzhom
31b8(phal chen): bar mos pas yongasu sngo'o// sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du gnas med par byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la gnas par mngon par mos pas yong su sngo'o// thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems rgya chen
32a1(phal chen): chung pa ma pa ma sa bsnam ma ma /  ma sa ra/  ma
32a2(phal chen): rig pas shin tu 'dzin pa'i mngon pa shes pas yo su sngo'o// rlom tha' dang dpung med cing chags pa med pas yong su sngo'o// lhag pa'i bsam pa rnam par dag pas yongasu sngo'o// 'gro ba thams cad la byams pa chen po spyod pas
32a3(phal chen): yongasu bsngo'o// snying rje chen po la rab tu brtson pa'i sems kyis yongasu bsngo'o// dga' ba'i sems kyis yongasu bsngo'o// btang snyoms kyis gnyis la chags pa dang bral ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba la dbang sgyur bar gnas pas yongasu
32a4(phal chen): sngo'o// rten cing 'brel te 'byung ba'i chos bsngags pa'i lam rab dbye bas chos rnam par dbye ba la zhugs pa dang / chos nyid la nges pa/ de gzhog pa'i yid dang sems kyis yongasu bsngo'o// dpal ba'i rgya
32a5(phal chen): mtshan gyi sems kyis yong su bsngo'o// gzhan gyis mi thub pa'i rgyu la mtshan dang ldan pa'i mdzod kyis yongasu bsngo'o// bdud rtsi dkyil 'khor thams cad rnam par gtor ba'i sems kyis yongs
32a6(phal chen): bsngo'o// rnam par dag pa dang chags pa med pa thams cad rab tu 'thob par bya ba'i sems kyis yong su bsngo'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad sbyang ba las phyir mi ldog par bya ba'i sems kyis yongasu bsngo'o// 
32a7(phal chen): chos dam pa dang rab dang phul la mngon par mos pa'i sems kyis yong su bsngo'o// yon tan gyi chos thams cad la dbang sgyur ba'i ye shes kyis khyad par du 'phags pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa la mos shing dang pa'i sems kyis/ 
32a8(phal chen): yo su sngo'o// bsam pa thams cad yong su rdzogs par bya ba dang / dungad kyi dkrugs ma thams cad rab tu gcig pa dang / chags pa med cing dri ma med pa'i chos kyi go 'bang 'thob pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi mangs 'gro ba thams
32b1(phal chen): cad la chos kyi 'khor lo bsko bskor ba las phyir mi ldog pa'i sems kyis yongasu bsngo'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos ye shes kyi nyi ma rab dang phul khyad par du 'phags pa'i 'od zer brgya stong gis brgyad pa'i chos rgya
32b2(phal chen): dbyings kyi ye shes chen po'i snang ba 'gro ba thams cad du rib tu dgye ba'i sems kyis yongasu bsngo'o// 'gro ba thams cad yongasu smin par bya zhing gdul ba dang / bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du sems kyi rgyud shin tu tshim par
32b3(phal chen): bya ba dang / sngon gyi smon lam chen po nub pa med pas phyi ma'i mtha'i mur spyod pa chen po'i rgyud rgyun mi 'chad cing rnam par dag pa dang / snang ba dri ma med pas rgyags pa dang dregs pa dang / nga rgyal shin tu gcad pa dang / 'gro
32b4(phal chen): ba thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa rnam par gtor ba dang / sred pa'i dra ba yang dag par gtugs pa dang / ma rig pa'i mun pa rdibs po bskul ba dang / bsgribs pa med cing dri ma dang bral la chags pa med pa'i chos kyi lo
32b5(phal chen): shin du legs pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad du bskal pa'i grangs na ma par 'chang ba med pas thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes rnam par 'tshang rgya ba dang / spyod pa'i rgyud las phyir mi ldog pas/ 
32b6(phal chen): sems can gyi tshogs so sor chags pa med pa'i ye shes rab dam pa mchog rnam par 'tshang rgya bar bya ba dang / sems can thams cad re re las sangs rgyas kyi sku shin tu bstan pa'i rnam par 'phral pa las phyir mi ldog
32b7(phal chen): par bya ba'i phyir yong su sngo'o// de ltar byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yong su sngo yang 'dod pa'i yul dang / khams gsum pa la gnas shing yong su mi bsngo ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar byang chub
32b8(phal chen): sems dpas ni dag pa'i rtsa ba rnams 'dod pags pas yongs su bsngo bar bya'o// byang chub sems dpas ni dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams zhe mi sdang bas yongasu bsngo bar bya'o// byang chub sems dpas ni dge ba'i rtsa
33a1(phal chen): rnams gti mug med pas yongasu bsngo ba dubya'o// byang chub sems dpas ni dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams gnod pa med pas yong su bsngo bar bya'o// byang chub sems dpas ni dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams nga rgyal
33a2(phal chen): med pas yongasu sngo ba bya'o// byang chub sems dpas ni dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams g.yo med pas yongasu bsngo bar bya'o// byang chub sems dpas ni dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams drang pos yongasu bsngo bar bya'o// byang chub sems dpas
33a3(phal chen): ni dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams rig pas yong su bsngo bar bya'o// byang chub sems dpas ni dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams mngon par brtson pas yong su bsngo bar bya ste/ de de ltar yo su bsngobs sems rab tu dang ba 'thob po// byang chub sebs
33a4(phal chen): dpa'i spyod pa la go skabs dbye ba 'thob po// byang chub sems rapa'i lam rnam par dag par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs/ su 'jug par 'gyuraro// sangs rgyas kyi ye shes rab tu 'grub par
33a5(phal chen): 'gyur ro// 'jig rten gyi nyes pa thams cad rab tu spong ngo // bdud rtsi las thams cad rab tu spong ngo // dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad rab tu dga' bar byed do// bdag gi smod lam chen po yongasu
33a6(phal chen): rdzogs par byed ngo // sems can thams cad gnyer ba chen pos shin tu 'bong ba yin no// gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos sbyin pas 'byung ba la sogs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag 'di ltar yongs
33a7(phal chen): sngo ste/ dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis sems can thams cad kyis chos kyi dbyings rnam par dag pa thob par gyur cig/ sems can thams cad kyis drabyangs snyad pa dang / ye shes kyi rnga'i dbyangs dang thams cad du bsam gyi khyab cing
33a8(phal chen): 'phags pa'i dbyangs dang / yid du 'ong ba'i dbyangs dang / dag pa'i dbyangs dang / zhing thams cad du spras rgyas par 'gengs pa'i dbyangs dang / yon tan bye ba brgya stong brjod du med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i dbyangs dang
33b1(phal chen): rnam po dang / sna rengs rnam par 'jug pa thams cad rab tu zhi ba byed pa'i byangs dang / chos kyi dbyings thams car smra rgyas par 'gengs pa'i dbyangs dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyis ngag mkhan po'i dbyangs rab tu thong bar gyur
33b2(phal chen): cig/ sems can thams cad kyis sgra dang dbyangs mtha' yas pa'i ye shes rab tu thob par gyur cig/ sgra dang dbyangs thams cad rnam par dag pa rab tu thob par gyur cig/ dbyangs tshad med pa dang / tshig gi lam thams cad shes
33b3(phal chen): parab tu thob par gyur cig/ dbyangs la dbang spyad ba zil gyis mi non pa'i dbyangs thams cad la rab tu 'jug pa'i ye shes rab tu thob par gyur cig/ dbyangs thams cad kyis brgyan pa'i dbyangs kyi yan lag rnam par dag pa'i
33b4(phal chen): dbyangs rab tu thob par gyur cig/ sems can thams cad 'gro ba thams cad kyis mnyan na mi ngoms pa'i dbyangs rab tu thob par gyur cig/ sems car thams cad kyis 'gro ba kun mos par nyan pa'i dbyangs kyi pha rol tu
33b5(phal chen): phyin pa thob par gyur cig/ sems can thams cad dad par byed pa/ 'i dbyangs dang ldan par gyur cig/ sems can thams cad sangs rgya sa kyi dbyangs su brjod pas smra ba'i sems dam par dag pa rab tu thob
33b6(phal chen): par gyur cig/ sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad rnam par sprog pa'i spang ba ring med pa'i dbyangs kyis smra bar gyur cig/ sems can thams cad chos thams cad kyi gzung kyi rgyar gyis chos thams cad rnam pa
33b7(phal chen): du ma bston pa dang / chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thob pa dang / bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i chos rdo rje'i tshig gis yang dag par bzung ba dang // chos nyid thams cad brjod pa rab tu dbye ba ye shes rang
33b8(phal chen): ldan pa dang / tshig dang yi ge brjod du med pa'i mdzod dang ldan pa dang / chos rnam pa tha dad pa thams cad shin tu bstan pa la gzhag pa dang / gnas par bya ba dang / rgyun mi 'chad par bya ba dang / chos snang ba thams cad
34a1(phal chen): kyi 'od rab tu thob pa la 'jug pa dang / 'gro ba rnams cad thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rnam par dag pa'i mthar thug pa med pa dang / chos thams cad kyis yang dag par bsdus pa'i don dang tshig dang / 
34a2(phal chen): yi ge rnam par 'phrul pa'i dbyangs kyi byin gyi brlabras dang ldan pa dang / chags pa med pa'i dbyangs la dbang pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa thob pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi shes pa'i dbyangs dang ldan par gyur cig/ dge ba'i rtsa ba
34a3(phal chen): 'dis sems can thams cad mi dma' ba'i dbyangs dang / bag tsha ba med pa'i dbyangs dang / 'dod chags med pa'i tshig gi dbyangs dang / ngag snyan pa'i dbyangs dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad mngon par dag
34a4(phal chen): bar byed pa'i dbyangs dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad brjod pa'i dbyangs dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi the tshom gcod cing khong du chud par byed pa'i dbyangs dang / spobs pas legs par sbyar ba'i dbyangs
34a5(phal chen): dang / sems can gnyid kyis log pa thams cad sad par byed pa'i/ dbyangs dam pa yangs pa dang ldan par gyur cig ces de ltar byangachub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag
34a6(phal chen): yongs su sngo'o// / bam po bzhi bcu rtsa bzhi po// gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag 'di ltar yongasu sngo ste/ sems can
34a7(phal chen): thams cad kyi lus rnam par dag cing kha na ma tho ba med pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi bsod nams rnam par dag cing kha na ma tho ba med pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi mtshan rnam par dag cing kha na ma tho ba med
34a8(phal chen): ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi las dang rnam par smin pa rnam par dag cing kha na ma tho ba med pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsam pa rnam par dag cing kha na ma tho ba med pa dang / sems
34b1(phal chen): can thams cad kyi byang chub kyi sems tshad med pa rnam par dag cing ban mtho ba med pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi dbang po'i tshul rab tu shes pa rnam par dag cing kha na ma tho ba med pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi mos pa
34b2(phal chen): rnam par dag cing kha na ma tho ba med pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi spyod pa chags pa med pa la brtson pa'i smon lam rnam par dag cing kha na ma tho ba med pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi dran pa dang / blo gros dang / rig
34b3(phal chen): pa dang / blo dang / ye shes ngam pa/ spobs pa rnam par dag cing kha na ma tho ba med pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yong su sngo ste/ sems can thams cad kyi lus rnam pa de
34b4(phal chen): lhar yongasu dag cing lus yongasu dag pa shin tu gsal brnyog pa med pa/ rnam par dang ba rnam par dag pa/ rdul med pa/ dri ma dang pra la ba 'od gsal zhing dang ba yid du 'ong ba/ bsgribs pa med pa
34b5(phal chen): de la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad gzugs brnyan gyi tshul du snang bar gyur cig/ mig yor gyi rnam par dmigs pas 'gro ba thams cad snang bar gyur cig/ mig yor gyi gnas kyi rnam
34b6(phal chen): pa thams cad snang bar gyur cig/ 'di lta ste dper na ma long gi dkyil 'khor shin tu dag pa la tshig su mi 'gyur bar gdong du dmigs pa rnam par snang ba de lta bu'i lus yongasu dag pa/ sems can thams cad kyis rab tu thob par
34b7(phal chen): gyur cig/ sems can thams cad byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yang dag par ston pa dang chos yang dag par ston pa dang / yon tan yang dag par ston pa dang / nan tan yang dag par ston pa dang / 'grub pa yang dag par ston pa
34b8(phal chen): dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod yul dang / smon lam yang dag par ston pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan na bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad yang dag par ston pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul
35a1(phal chen): pa dang / cho 'phrul yang dag par ston pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i byin gyi brlabs yang dag par ston pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa
35a2(phal chen): dang / smon lam yongasasu rdzogs pas thams cad mkhyen pa yang dag par ston par gyur cig/ de ltar yong su dag pa'i lus kyi rnam pas sems can thams cad ma lus par yongasu bzung ste/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams kyi
35a3(phal chen): sku yongasasu dag pa dang ldan par gyur cig/ gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos kyi sbyin pas 'byung ba la sogs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag 'di ltar yongasu sngo ste/ dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis 'jig rten gyi khams
35a4(phal chen): thams cad du rjesu song ba'i lus kyis byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod par gyur cig/ 'gro ba thams cad kyis blta na don yod cing byang chub kyi sems las phyir mi ldog pa dang / sems can thams cad la 'thun
35a5(phal chen): par gyur pas/ bsam pa mi 'khrugs pa dang / bskal pa thams cad du skye ba med par byung bas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du ma 'ongs pa'i dus kyi phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug par gnas pa dang / chos kyi
35a6(phal chen): dbyings tshad med par snying rje chen po rgyun mi gcod pas/ sems can thams cad la dus la bab par chos ston pa mi gtong bas dbang po yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhon du shes pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen dran pa'i khongs su gtogs
35a7(phal chen): pa'i sems dang ldan pas/ sems bskyed pa gcig dang yang mi 'dral ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad 'dod cing zhal blta ba'i sems kyis de bzhin gshegs pa yid la byed pa mi gtang ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba brtsams pa thams
35a8(phal chen): cad rjes med par mi byed cing / sems can thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems la rab tu dgod pa'i sems kyi phyir mi ldog pa'i 'khor lo thod par bya ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi chos snang ba thams cad kyis chos thams
35b1(phal chen): da la lnga ning sems pa mang dag par med pas chos kyi sprid yang dag par 'dzin pa'i byin kyi bras kyis byang chub sems dpa'i spyang baspyod par gyur cig/ sems can thams cad 'ag pa dang / mi bams cad la 'jug pa dang / chos
35b2(phal chen): thams cad la 'jug pa dang / 'jig rten dang dus thams cad la 'jug pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi las dang rnam par smin pa shes pa la 'jug pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad thangs mkhas pa'i ye shes la 'jug pa
35b3(phal chen): ngang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi mdzong bar bsgrub pa'i ye shes la 'jug pa dang / byang chub sengs dpa' thams cad kyi rnam par dag pa'i spyod yul gyi ye shes la 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas thangs cad kyi byin gyi brlabs dang /

41a1(phal chen): rgyan brjod dumed pa'i yang byed du med bkun nas gnas par gyur cig ces bya ba nas/ mong bu rin po che bams cad kyi ming kun tu bres pa'i rong du rin po mo'i gang rnam par dag pa yong du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa
41a2(phal chen): kun nas gnas par gyur cig/ de ltar tshul de ltar de bzhin du kun tu byas te dmigs pa re re zhing lan brgyar bzlas par bya'o// ye shes kyi nor bu rin po che chags pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i yid kyi las kyi ye shes kyi nor bu ring po
41a3(phal chen): me rnam par dag pa brjod med pa'i yang brjod med pa'i bar du gnas par gyur cig ces de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos kyi sbyin pa la sogs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyis bsgrubs pa'i
41a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing yong su dag par yong su sngo'o// sems can thams cang yong su dag pa mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir yongasu sngo'o// sem sa can thams cad mnyam pa nyid mi 'khrugs pa yongasu dag pa dang / 
41a5(phal chen): sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi chos zab mo la 'jug pa dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyi da kyi phyir/ bsod nams kyi stobs thub pa med brdam par dag pa dang / 
41a6(phal chen): sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ bsod nams kyi mtshan nyid rnam par dag bzil gyis mngon pa bstan pa dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ mi zad pa'i ye shes kyi stobs kyis sems can ba
41a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi chos la gzung ba dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ tshig gi rnam grangs meng ba shim tu ngag pa'i dbyangs dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ thogs pa med pa'i mig
41a8(phal chen): gis chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa mamakha'i mthas gtugs pa shes par bya ba dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ sngon gyi mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'byar klas
41b1(phal chen): pa thams cad rjesu drang ba rnam par dag pa dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ bsgribs pa med pa'i blo gros chen pos chos nges par rtogs pa'i mdzod dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ byang chub
41b2(phal chen): mtha' dang dpung med pas chos kyi dbyings rgyas par dgang ba la chags pa med par yang dag par gzhol ba dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur pas rnam par
41b3(phal chen): dbye ba med pa dang / sems cad thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur pa'i lus kyi las dang / ngag gi las dang / yid kyi las yon tan thams cad kyi rgyan pa rnam par dag pa dang / sems
41b4(phal chen): bams ca sa ma kyi tu byid/ kun tu bzang ma myong kyi tshul gcigs gyur pas 'byung bdang / sems pan thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyid/ sa ma rgyam gyi'i sems cad chud kyi tshul
41b5(phal chen): cing rnam par dge pa la 'jug pa dang / goms par bya ba dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ shes pa tham sa cad rnam par dpyad pa la 'jug pa yongasasu rdzogs par bya ba dang / 
41b6(phal chen): sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ mi mnyam pa med par dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su bsngo ba dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ lhag pa'i bsam pa gcig ras gcig tu brgyud
41b7(phal chen): pa rnam pa tha dad pas thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yongasu rdzogs par bya ba dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ dka' bo'i phyogs thams cad bsgrub cing brtan par bya ba dang / sems can thams
41b8(phal chen): cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ skad cig gcig gis thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du mngon bar 'tshang rgya ba'i mthar thug par bya ba dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir/ nan tan gyi rnam pa thams cad yongs su/ 
42a1(phal chen): rdzogs pa rab par dag pa yong su bsgrub pa'i phyir yongasu sngo ste/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' cher pos// dge ba'i rtsa bde dag sems ca mnyam pa nyid kyi phyi/ yongasu bsngos da
42a2(phal chen): chos thams cad yongasu dag par chos bsrur ba'i tshul gyis chos nyid kyi stobs mnyam pa nyid yongasu rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir yongasu sngo ste/ dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis chos rgya mtsho brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa 'thob padas pa
42a3(phal chen): dag pa'i spyod pa'i byin gyi brlabs dang ldan par gyur cig ces yong su sngo'o// chos rgya mtsho de dag las chos rgya mtsho re re zhing yang chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa'i ye shes kyi snang ba rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir yongasu sngo'o// tshig
42a4(phal chen): thams cad rab tu dbye bas shin tu bstan pa mngon par bsgrub pa yang par bstan pa'i phyir yong su sngo'o// chos 'byam zas pa mtha' ngaHnga med pa thams cad dang / chos kyi snang ba thams cad kyi ting nge 'dzin
42a5(phal chen): rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir yongasu sngo'o// dus gsum dang mi 'ag la ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi spobs pa thob par bya ba'i phyir yongs su sngo'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba de 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang
42a6(phal chen): da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i lus thob par bya ba'i phyir yongasu sngo'o// dge ba'i ba'i rtsa ba de sangs rgyas la dga' ba dang / chos la dga' ba dang / sems can thams cad yongasu bskyab
42a7(phal chen): ba'i phyir/ snying rje chen po la dga' ba las phyir mi ldog pa yongasu rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir yong su sde'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba de las kyi rnam pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa la bsgribs pa med pa'i ye shes kyis yang dag par gzhol
42a8(phal chen): bya ba dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa thams cad kyi sems dang dbang po dang bar bya ba dang / dga' bar bya ba'i phyir yong su sngo'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba de zhing gi rgyud snrel zhi ngag/ spyi ru tshugasu rgyu 'a thams cad shin tu/ 
42b1(phal chen): bstan pa dang / phra ba dang rgya ba dang / yangs pa dang / dog pa dang / thagru che ba sna tshogs dang / rnam par dag pa dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa thams cad du chos kyi 'khor lo rgyun mi 'chad par mnyam pa nyid du yang dag par skor ba
42b2(phal chen): phyir yong su sde'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba de sems bskyed pa'i skad cig re re dang / mi 'jigs pa gzhan dang gzhan tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa mi zad pas/ chos sdang ba sar pa/ gsar pa rab tu thob cing bstan pa dang bshad pa'i
42b3(phal chen): phyir yongasasu bsngo'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba de dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad tshol ba la lhag pa'i bsam pa dang / dbang po ma 'khrugs shing mi dpa' bas/ chos 'jam klas pa thams cad ma lus par mngon par shes pa'i ye shes dang
42b4(phal chen): chos kyi rdzu 'phrul thob pas/ sems cad gyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor las klas pa thams cad mngon par dga' ba dang / tshim par chos thams cad rab tu bstan pa'i phyir yong su sngo'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba de chos kyi dbyings tshang
42b5(phal chen): med pa thams cad du song ba'i yong su bsngo ba la gnas shing 'di lhar yongasu sngo ste/ chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song ba'i lus/ kyi las kyis yongasu sngo'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song ba'i
42b6(phal chen): ngag gi las kyi yongasu sngo'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song ba'i yid kyi las kyis yongasu sde'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song ba'i ge thugs mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yong su sde'o// chos kyi dbyings cang
42b7(phal chen): med par song ba'i tshor ba dang / 'du shes dang / 'du byed dang / rnam par shes pa mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yong su sngo'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song ba'i phung po mnyam panyid la gnas shing yongasu sngo'o// 
42b8(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song ba'i khams mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yong su sde'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song ba'i skye mched mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yongasu sngo'o// chos kyi dbyings tshar reng bar song ba'i rang
43a1(phal chen): mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yongasu sde'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song ba'i phyi rol mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yongasu sngo'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song ba'i brtsam pa mnyam pa nyid la
43a2(phal chen): gnas shing yong su sde'o// chos kyi dbyings tshang med par song ba'i bsam pa mnyam pa nyid la gangs shing yong su sde'o// chos kyi dbyings ma med par song ba'i sbyor ba mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yong su sde'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song
43a3(phal chen): ba'i mos pa mnyam pa nyid la gangs shing yongasu sngo'o// chos kyi dbyings tshang med par song ba'i dbang po mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yongasu sde'o// chos kyi dbyings tshang med par song ba'i sdong gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha' dang / nga ltar
43a4(phal chen): byung ba mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yongasu sde'o// chos kyi dbyings tsha med par song ba'i las kyi rnam par smi ba mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yongasu bsngo'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song ba'i kur ras
43a5(phal chen): nyon mongs pa dang // rnam par byang ba rnam par dag pa mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yongasu sngo'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song ba/ 'i sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yongasu sngo'o// 
43a6(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings tshang med par song ba'i zhing thams cad mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yong su sngo'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song ba'i chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yongasu sngo'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par
43a7(phal chen): song ba'i 'gro ba thams cad du snang bamanyam pa nyid la gnas shing yongasu sngar// chos kyi dbyings chang med par song ba'i byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yongasu sngo'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par
43a8(phal chen): song ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / spong las thams cad mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yong su bsngo'o// chos kyi dbyibyis tshang med par song ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'byung ba thams cad mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing
43b1(phal chen): so su sde'o// chos kyi dbyings cang med par dong ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i yong su sming bar bya ba dang / 'dul ba thams cad mnyam pa nyid la gangs shing yo su stso'o/ chos kyi dngas tshang med par song ba'i byang dub sems dpa'i
43b2(phal chen): 'khor thams cad mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yongasu sde'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song ba'i chos thams cad mi gnyis pa'i mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yong su sngo'o// chos kyi dbyings tshad med par song ba'i de bzhin gsheg
43b3(phal chen): ba'i dkyil 'khor thams cad mnyam pa nyid la gnas shing yong su sde'o// de de ltar yongasu sngo bas chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa dang / mnyam pa'i lus yongasu dag pa kun nas gnas par 'gyur ro// chos kyi dbyings tshang med pa dang
43b4(phal chen): mnyam pa'i ngag yong su dag pa kun nas gnas par 'gyur ro// chos/ kyi dbyings tshad med pa dang mnyam pa'i sems yongasu dag par kun nas gnas par 'gyur ro// chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa dang mnyam
43b5(phal chen): ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / spod lam yongasu dag pa kun nas gnas par 'gyur ro// chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa dang mnya ma ba'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yongasu dag bkur nas gnas par 'gyura'o// 
43b6(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa dang mnyam pa'i chos thams cad bstam pa dang brjod pas byang chub sems dpa' thams cad go bar bya ba yong su dag pa kun nas gnas par 'gyur ro// chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa dang mnyam pa'i
43b7(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par chos kyi dbyings la yang dag par gzhol ba'i tshul gyis lus 'byam klas brjesu 'gro bar kun nas gnas par 'gyur ro// chos kyi dbyings chang med pa dang mnyam pa'i chos snga
43b8(phal chen): bamatha' dang shud med pa thams cad dang / mi 'jigs pa rnam par dag pa'i tshig gcig brjod pa sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi the tshom gcod cing / sems dang dbang po dang / bsam pa khong du chud par
44a1(phal chen): byed pas tshim par byed pa dang / bla na med pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i stob dang / mi 'jigs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phral ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi che ba nyid dang / ye shes la
44a2(phal chen): 'jug pa shim tu 'phags pa dang / chos mngon par shes pa la gnas par bya ba kun nas gnas par 'gyur te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi yongasu bsngo ba chos kyi dbyings
44a3(phal chen): tshad med pa zhes bya ba bcu pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i chos smin pa la sogs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad bsngo ba des yongasasu bsngo ba des yongasu bsngos na/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i
44a4(phal chen): spyod pa dang / smod lam mtha' dang dpung med pa yongasu rdzogs pa 'thobapar 'gyur ro// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing chos kyi dbyings kyi klas pa namakha'i mthas gtugs bzang
44a5(phal chen): yong su dag pa thob par 'gyur ro// sems can thams cad kyis kyang / rab tu thob par bya ba la brtson par byed par 'gyuraro// chos tha mas cad la 'jug pa'i ye shes mtha' dang dbung med pa thams
44a6(phal chen): cad yongasu 'grub par 'gyur ro// sems bskyed pa mtha' dbang bud med pa thams cad kyi skad cig re re la sangs rgyas skyed pa thams cad mthong ba rab tu thob cing khong du chud par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs
44a7(phal chen): pa thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul ba dang / rgya chen po'i rnam par 'phral ba dang / bsgribs pa med pa'i rnam par 'phral pa dang / bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad rnam par dag par
44a8(phal chen): byed pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad byin gyis rlab cing brtan par byed pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / shin tu bstan pa brjod du med pa'i rnam par 'phral ba dang / dus thams cad du rnam par 'brun
44b1(phal chen): pa'i mngon pa shes pa dang / ye shes dang phyir mi ldog sa'i byin gyis brlabs kyis chos kyi dbyings mtha' dbang bud med pa thams cad ma lus par rgyas par 'gengs pa la 'jug cing khong du chud par 'gyur ro// kun tu bzang
44b2(phal chen): po'i mig mtha' dang dbung med pa mngon par bsgrubs pa yong su rdzogs pa 'thob par 'gyur ro// mtha' dbang dbung med pa'i chos bstan pa chags pa med pa'i rna ba'i ye shes khong du chud pa yang dag par 'dzin par 'gyuraro/ 
44b3(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbung med pa thams cad lus kyi skyil mo dkrungs gcig gis yongasu rgyas par byin gyis rlob kyang sems can thams cad la gnod pa med par byed par 'gyur ro// dus gsum mtha' dang dpung
44b4(phal chen): med pa thams cad la 'jug pa'i ye shes 'khyam klas pa mo su rdzogs dpa 'thob cing khong du chud par 'byung ngo // blo mtha' dang dbung med pa thams cad rnam par dag pa dang / sems can thams cad rnam
44b5(phal chen): bar dag pa dang / chos thams cad rnam par dag pa dang / skye mched yongasu shes pa'i ye shes thams cad rnam par dag pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings mtha' dang dpung med pa thams cad
44b6(phal chen): la 'jug cing rgyas par 'gengs pa'i ye shes rnam par dag pa dang / sems can gyi ris dang / skye gnas rnam pa sna tshogs su gyur pa thams cad nas byung ba'i sgra dang / smra ba dang / skad thams cad ma lus pa la mngor sum gyi ye shes
44b7(phal chen): rnam par dag pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par rnam pa mtha' yas pa'i 'od zer dang / 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu gtong zhing mtha' dang dpung med pa snang bar byed pa rnam par dag pa dang / dus gsum thams
44b8(phal chen): tsang kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa ma lus par mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes rnam par dag pa dang / 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / nga ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i dkyil 'khor mtha' dang dpung med pa ma lus pa thams cad
45a1(phal chen): la skad cig gcig tu 'jug pa'i ye shes rnam par dag pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi mngon par 'du bya ba thams cad ma lus pa la 'jug pas 'gro ba thams cad dang dbung med pa rnam par dag par bya ba rab
45a2(phal chen): tu thob par 'gyur ro// yong su rdzogs par byed pa'o// rab tu sgrub bo// rnam par dag par byed do// mnyam par byed do// mngon sum du byed do// rab tu rtogs par byed do// khong du chud par byed do// yang dag par sems par byeda'o// rnam
45a3(phal chen): par dag pa thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa thob par bya ba rjes su thob par byed do// de nas de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten du/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya phrag stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig
45a4(phal chen): rten gyi khams rnam pa drug tu g.yos te/ g.yos so// rab tu g.yos so// kun tu g.yos so// 'gul to// rab tu 'gul to// kun tu 'gul to// ldeg go// rab tu ldeg go// kun tu ldeg go// 
45a5(phal chen): chem chem/ rab tu chem chem/ kun tu che ma chem mo// lung 'ur/ rab tu 'ur 'ug/ kun tu 'u 'ur ro// shig shig/ rab tu shig shi ga/ kun tu shig shig go// sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / chos nyid
45a6(phal chen): rab tu thob pas lha rdzas kyi me tog gi sprin gyi char mngon par bab bo// lha rdzas kyi phreng ba'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab bo// lha rdzas kyi phye ma'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab bo// lha rdzas kyi gos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab bod/ 
45a7(phal chen): lha rdzas kyi rin po che'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab bo// lha rdzas kyi lhab lhub kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab bo// lha rdzas kyi spos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab bo// lha rdzas kyi nor bu rin po che'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab bo// 
45a8(phal chen): lha rdzas kyi dus dang 'thun pa'i tsan dan gyi sprin gyi char mngon par 'babo// lha rdzas kyi sprul gyi snying po'i tsan dan mchog gi sprin gyi char mngon par rababo// lha rdzas kyi gdugs dang rgyal mtshan dang ba dan kha dog sna tshogs kyi sprin
45b1(phal chen): gyi chal mngon par bab po// lha rdzas kyi lha'i lus grangs med pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab bo// lha rdzas kyi dbyangs kyi yan lag brgya stong brjod du med pa'i tshig dang / brjod pa la rtog pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa/ yid du
45b2(phal chen): 'ong bar spyod pa'i chos chen po'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po// lha rdzas kyi de bzhin gshegs pas bstod pa'i sangs rgyas bsngags pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po// lha rdzas kyi legs so// zhes bya ba dang / 
45b3(phal chen): lhung lhung ldegs kyi sgra 'byin pa dang / dga' bar byed pa'i dbyangs kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab bo// lha rdzas kyi lha'i lus bye ba khrag khrig brgya grangs med cing brjod du med pas rab tu btung ngo // lha yul gyi lha grangs med pa sangs rgyas
45b4(phal chen): rjes su dran pa la brtson par yid la byed cing de bzhin gshegs pa la shin tu dad pa'i sems kyi rgyud dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang mi 'bral ba'i sems kyis mngon par gnas so// lha rdzas kyi rol
45b5(phal chen): mo brdung ba dang / dkrol ba'i sgra lha'i glu'i dbyangs kyi tshul grangs med par grag pa de bzhin gshegs pa mchod cing yid la bya ba la brtson pa rnams kyang rab tu bsgrags so// lha rdzas shin tu 'das pa'i
45b6(phal chen): 'od zer brgya stong grangs med pas kyang 'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ na mkha'i mthas gtugs pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi thag gru thams cad du rab tu snang bas khyab par byas so// lha
45b7(phal chen): rdzas las 'das pa'i sprul pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi yul grangs med pa bstan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgra'i cho 'phrul rnams kyang yang dag par bstan par gyur to// gling bzhi pa 'di dga' ldan gyi gnasu lha'i dbang
45b8(phal chen): po rab dga' ldan gyi khang pa na ji lta ba de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du yang phyogs bcu rgyas par bal de zhing chos bstan pa 'di nyid kun tu byung ngo // sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i
46a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi pha rol ngag nas kyang / sangs rgyas rgyas kyi zhing durgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul shing tu phra ba snyed kyi byang chub sems dpa' lcags ras phye
46a2(phal chen): bcu bkang sde 'di skad zer ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de ltar khyod kyis yongasu bsngo ba'i chos nyid 'di bshad pa legs so legs so// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ bdag cag kun kyang ming rdo rje rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba sha stag ste/ 'jig cer
46a3(phal chen): gyi khams kyi ming rje rje'i 'od ces bya ba dag ma de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshar rdo rje dpal zhes bya ba bsugs pa ngag gis drung nas 'dir phyin te/ kun na yang sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis 'khor gyi rnam pa 'di lta bu dag na/ tshig 'di dag
46a4(phal chen): dang / yi ge 'di dag dang / go bar bya ba'i de ngag gis don 'di nyid lhag pa med cing chang ba med par brjod de chos 'di nyid stong to// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ bdag cag kyang de ltar phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi
46a5(phal chen): khams re re'i gling bzhi pa dag gi dga' ldan gyi gnas kyi lha'i rgyal po rab dga' ldan gyi khang pa rim po che thams cad kyi rgyan ces bya bangag tu sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul shing tu phra
46a6(phal chen): bsnyed kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnams phyin pa mngon du mthong pa sha stag sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis 'khor 'dir phyin to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan gyis phyogs bcu bltas te/ 'khor thams cad
46a7(phal chen): la bltas nas chos kyi dbyings la rnam par blta ba dang / don dang tshig dang yi ge la rab tu 'jug pa dang / sems bskyed pa mtha' dang dpung med par yangs pa yongasu sgom pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad la snying rje chen po khyab
46a8(phal chen): par bya ba dang / dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi rigs su sems yang dag par 'brel par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yon tan la 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyis brlabs pa'i lus
46b1(phal chen): yang dag par bskyed pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa yang dag par shes par bya ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa'ang ji ltar dus la bab pa la yang dag par blta ba dang / chos kyi lus kyi rjesu song ba'i gzugs
46b2(phal chen): kyi lus yang dag par bstan par byed cing / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// de dag chos la rab tu mkhas gyur cing // chos rgyud mtha' yas rnam par dag byas nas/ 
46b3(phal chen): chos kyi 'od byed chos la kha lo sbyar/ chos rnams rab rtogs chags pa red pa thob// de dag chos kyi kha lo sbyar gyur te// shin tu dkon pa'i chos rnams stod byed cing // chos kyi sgo la rab tu gzhag bya bar/ sems
46b4(phal chen): can mtha' yas phyogs su go bar byed// de dag chos kyi gang cher mtsho 'thung zhing // chos nyid spri char pogs su rab tu 'bebs// 'ji garten khams su chos nyid nyi shar cing / sems cad par phyir
46b5(phal chen): chos rnams stong pa byed/ de dag shin tu dkon pa'i sprin bdag ste/ chos kyi rnam tshul shes pa rjesu thob// chos kyi snang bas rab tu sems gsal ba/ 'jigs med 'jig rten dag tu chos
46b6(phal chen): rab stod/ shin tu dri med chos kyi sems dang ldan// chos kyi sgo la de dag rab tu gnas/ spro rnams rgya mtsho de dag shin tu 'phags// 'jig rten dag tu chos nyid rnga yang rdung // de dag shing tu dkor pa'i chos
46b7(phal chen): brjod cing / chos nyid bsod nams yang dag spogs par byed// chos nyid bsam pa yongasu dag byed cing // chos kyi gter rnams 'gro ba kun la ston// chos kyi khang par rgyal bas dbang bskur ba// chos nyid
46b8(phal chen): ye shes snying po'i lus dang ldan// chos kyi mtshan gzhi rtogs pa'i ye shes can// de dag chos nyid bzang po'i chos la gnas// rgyal ba kun gyis gang la bstod mdzad dang / rab kyi bul gyis gang zhig sa/ 
47a1(phal chen): 'gyur cing // skyes dbang thams cad gang gis bskyed gyur pa'i// sbyid pa dam pade dag sbyid par byed// de dag chos kyi lus ldang shes dang ldan// 'jig rten mkhas pas chos nyid sprul mdzad dang / 
47a2(phal chen): chos kyi sgron ma 'gro la phan pa'i phyir// dma' ba med par mtha' yas chos ston to// de dag chos bzang ngam pa sbrid byas nas// dge rtsa de dag rjesu sems byed cing // 'jig rten dag tu dge ba gang byas pa// de dag yongs
47a3(phal chen): bsngo'i shes dang ldan pa yin// rang byung thams cad gang gis bskyed gyur pa'i// dge rtsa de dag 'gro ba'i don du shes// thams cad rnam phye rnam par dag gyur cig/ sangs rgyas rgyan gyi pha rol phyin par byed/ zhing gi rgyan
47a4(phal chen): mang shin tu rgya che zhing / phyogs rnams kun tu de la tshad med pa sa// 'jig rten kun tu bsam yas rgyar ldan pa// de 'dra zhing rnams ma lus kur gyur cig/ skyes bu 'dul ba'i ye shes
47a5(phal chen): ji tsam pa// de 'drar sems can rnams ngag ldar gyur te/ rgyal ba'i sras po bzang po ji bzhid du/ yon tam kun gyis sems brgyan ldan gyur cig/ de dag rnam 'phrul shin tu rnam yang
47a6(phal chen): pa// gang gis 'jig rten ma lus rgyas gang ba// de'i spyod la shes rab bzang gnas par// sems can thams cad ma lus gyur par shog/ ji snyed 'jig rten ma lus gang yang rung // phyogs su rgyal ba kun gyis
47a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas pa// kun kyang kun tu bzang po ji bzhin du// legs spyod ngas pa mchog dang ldar gyur cig/ yon tan rgyud rnams ji snyed gang yang rung // rgyal sras rnams dang rgyal bas thugs chud pa'i// yon tan
47a8(phal chen): bang la mtha' dbang dbung med pa// yon tan de 'drar sems can kur gyur cig/ gang yang rdzu 'phrul stobs dang ldan pa'i rnams// 'jug pa kun la bslab pa kun bslabs pa// rnam 'phrul thams cad yang dag sngon
47b1(phal chen): pa'i rnams// phyogs rnams thams cad rgyas par ra gyur cig/ sems kyi skad cig gcig gis rang byung rnams// 'dren pa sems can kun dang mnyam mthong ste/ chos rnams thams cad ma lus bsdu byas shing // skra rtse
47b2(phal chen): gcig du mi mgon sdud gyur cig/ 'jig rten 'di na 'gro ba gang rgyu ba// gang rnams mi'i dam pas mkhyen gyur pa// de dang mnyam pa thams cad ma lus pa'i// 'jig rten mkhyen la mchod pa byed gyur cig/ spos kyi
47b3(phal chen): rgyud dang de bzhin me tog dang // gos kyi rgyud dang de bzhin gdugs rnams kyis// chos dbyings ma lus rgyas par gang byas shing // 'jig rten kun tu yid kyis 'gengs gyur cig/ sangs rgyas mtshan gyi rnam pa
47b4(phal chen): bsam yas pa// skra rtse gcig tu sangs rgyas bsdu ba yis/ lhag ma med par lam rnams ku bsdus shing // 'jig rten sprod la phyag 'tsha' gyur bar shog/ rgyal ba de dag kun la phyag
47b5(phal chen): 'tshal te// thams cad lus kyi tshul gyis 'dud byed cing / phyogs rnams kun tu rgyal ba kun sto pas// phyi ma'i bskal kur zad par byed gyur cig/ sems can snyed kyi yid
47b6(phal chen): kyi rnam pa yis// rgyal ba gcig la'ang mchod pa byed gyur cig/ ji ltar rgyal ba gcig mchod de bzhin du// skyes dbang ma lus kun la'ang mchod gyur cig/ de dag mchod pa'i yon tam brjod byed pas/ 
47b7(phal chen): 'gro ba kun du bskal bzang gyur kyang // skyes bu 'dul ba dpe zla med pa yi// rgyal ba mchod pa'i mthar thug med gyur cig/ 'gro ba kun na bskal mang ji snyed pa// de snyed bskal pa spyad pa spyod byed cing // rgyal
47b8(phal chen): ba gcig la rim gro bya bas kyang // bskal po thams cad ma lus zad gyur cig/ rgyal ba gcig la ji tsam brjod gyur pa/ rgyal ba kun la'ang bskal pa de snyed de/ bskal pa'i grangs kyi mthar thug pa gyur cig
48a1(phal chen): rgyal ba'i spyod pas spro ba med gyur cig/ ji ltar chos dbyings rnam par dag pa dang / ji tsam rgya chen yongasu mtha' yas pa// de snyed rgya chen me tog bzang po'i rnams// thub rang sems can
48a2(phal chen): snyeng la 'bum gyur cig/ dri zhim ldan pa'i de bzhin phye ma dag/ gtsang zhing rnam dag rnam pa sna tshogs la// 'gro ba kun na dpe zlang dmigs med pa// de 'dras rgyal ba mchod pa byed gyur cig/ zhing rnams
48a3(phal chen): du ma sems cad mnyam pa yi// rgyal ba gcig la gdugs rnams 'bul byed cing // rgyal ba kun la'ang de bzhin dag pa bya bas// rgyal ba rnams la gdugs mchod byed gyur cig/ byug pa dam pa mchog
48a4(phal chen): tu gyur pa rnams// 'gro ba 'di na gang la dpe med pa// de yis sangs rgyas mchod byed spyod pa yis// bskal mang sems can mnyam bzang gyur cig/ de bzhin byug dang spos kyi phye ma dang // me tog
48a5(phal chen): bdug pa na bza' spos rnams dang / rin chen lhang lhub mchod pa mtha/ 'ayas pa'i// rim gro skyo ba med par byed gyur cig/ 'jig rte/ na sgron ma sems can mnyam padag/ skad cig re rer byang chub
48a6(phal chen): 'chang rgya ba// de dag yon tan mtha' yas brjod byed cing // skyes bu 'dul la mchod pa byed gyur cig/ sems can mnyam pa'i 'jig rten me khyen pa la// sems can mnyam pa'i bskal pa bzang byas shing / 
48a7(phal chen): blo mchog ldan pa mchod pa byed pa ni// rgyal bas bshad kyang zad par ma gyur cig/ rgyal ba rnams la 'di 'dra'i mchod byed cing / sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul kun tu 'gengs byed pas// bzang dang ldan pa'i spyod kha gnas/ 
48a8(phal chen): bcas shing // sangs rgyas ma lus thams cad mthong gyur cig/ 'gro kun dge ba ji snyed yod pa dang / byas dang byed gyur de bzhin byed pa dag/ bzang po ci bzhin de 'dra'i sa dag la// kun kyang kun nas bzang por
48b1(phal chen): reng gyur cig/ 'jig rten thams cad ma lus sems can rnams// ji snyed rgyal bkun gyis zhugs chung pa// kun kyang mkhas pa kun gyis sngags pa yi// kun tu bzang po'i de bzhin 'gyur bar shog/ phyogs rapas ma lus
48b2(phal chen): kun tu ji byas pa/ skyes bu dam pa de ltar yongasu bsngo// rdo rje'i rgyal mtsham rgyal bas sungs pa// yongasu bsngo dam pa mchog dang phul yang yin// de bzhin zhing rnams thams cad ma lus par// rgyu bzhin kun kyang
48b3(phal chen): khong du chud bya ste// sems can ji snyed thams cad ma lus pa// de dag kun kyang kun tu bzang gyur cig/ sbyin pas yongs sngo ji bzhin reng gyur cig/ tshul khrims kyis kyang bsngo bzhin red gyur cig/ brtson 'grus
48b4(phal chen): spobs kyis bskal par mi ldog cing / bzod pas 'khrugs pa med pa'i yid gyur cig/ bsam gtan gyis kyang rtse gcig yid lnga na zhing // ting 'dzin kun gyi spyod yul shes gyur cig/ shes rab
48b5(phal chen): dus rnams gsum po thams cad du/ 'jig rten dag tu mthar dang gas med gyur cig/ lus dang ngag dang yid rnams thams cad kyang // rnam pa kun tu rnam dag mkhas gyur cig/ spyod
48b6(phal chen): pa de dag thams cad ma lus par/ kun kyang kun tu bzang por reng gyur cig/ ji ltar chos dbyings rlom pa'i sems med cing // de la spros dang chags pa med pa dang // mya ngan 'da' dang ba sgrings pa med pa ltar/ 
48b7(phal chen): bzhing sems la rloms sems med gyur cig/ chos mkhas yong su bsngo ba gang brjod pa// de ni rgyal bas gsungs pa'i bsngo ba ste/ mkhas pa'i spyod pa ji nas 'grub 'gyur bar// dge ba yangs pa de yis yongasu
48b8(phal chen): bsngo// rgyal ba'i sras kyis 'di la bslab bya ste// ji snyed gang yong thams cad ma lus par// khams rnams kun kyang yongasu bsdu byas te/ ci nas bde gshegs stobs la 'jug par bsngo// yangs paji
49a1(phal chen): steng rgyal bas gsungs pa dang // kun tu bzang zhes gang la gdags pa'i// rgyal ba'i sras rnams gang la gnas gyur pa'i// spyod padam pa de dag su 'dod pas// sems can ma lus thams cad bkra
49a2(phal chen): bar nus// dus gsum sems kyang ma lus kun bgrang nus// gang la kun tu bzang por ming gdags pa// rgyal sras de yi yon tan mtha' med do// nam mkha' sbra rtses bgrang bar nus kyang srid// zhing rnams kun gyi rdul kyang
49a3(phal chen): bgrang bar rung // gang la rgyal sras drang srong che gnas pa'i// spyod pa de dag bgrang bar mi nus so// chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa zhes bya ba ste/ yongs su bsngo ba bcu pa'o// shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ 
49a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las/ rdo rje rgyal mtsham gyis so ngas su bsngo ba'i le'u ste sumacu'o// / bam po bzhi bcu rtsa lnga pa// de nas bcom ldan
49a5(phal chen): 'das lha'i rgyal po dbang sgyur gyi gnas kyi nong bu rin po chengs par/ khang pa na/ byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun chen po thams cad kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi
49a6(phal chen): ldog pa 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan dang / gzhan nas 'dus pa sha su// kun kyang / byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi yul dang spyod yul thams cad rab tu thob pas gnas pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye
49a7(phal chen): shes kyi yul la 'jug cing gzhol ba'i spyod yul ma gtang ba 'gro ba thams cad yongasu smin par bya ba dang / gdul bar bya ba'i dus bzhin du thogs pa med pa'i byin gyi brlabs rnam pa tha dad pas bya ba thams cad yang
49a8(phal chen): dag par smon pa la mkhas pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam thams cad mngon par bsgrub cing bskal pa dang / shing dang dus su spyong ba la gnas pa'i rgyun mi gcod pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i bsod nams dang / 
49b1(phal chen): ye shes dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi tshogs yongasasu rdzogs shing 'gro ba thams cad nye bar 'tsho ba mi zad pa la rab tu zhugs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i shes rab dang / thabs thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dam pa thob pa/ byang
49b2(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i spyod pas 'khor ba dang / mya ngan las 'das pa'i sgo yang dag par bstan cing // shin tu bslab pa'i rgyun mi gcod pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / 
49b3(phal chen): ting 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa dang / mngon par shes pa dang / rig pa dang / ye shes la rnam par rol pa'i mngon par shes pas bya ba thams cad yang dag par ston pa la mkhas pa/ byang chub sems
49b4(phal chen): dba'i rdzu 'phrul dang / spobs dang / dbang thams cad thob cing mngon par 'du bya ba med pa'i sems skad cig gis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor 'dong ba la
49b5(phal chen): sngon du 'dren pa'i gtam gyi skyes bu dam pa/ de bzhin gshen/ sa pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo yang dag par gzung ba dang / sangs rgyas la mchod pa dang / rim gro rgya chen
49b6(phal chen): bo bya ba'i don du mngon par brtson pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i las thams cad yang dag par blang ba mnyam pa nyid kyis sbyor bas/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du lus kyi gzugs brnyan rab tu
49b7(phal chen): 'byung ba/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du chags pa med pa'i dbyangs rab tu sgrog pas/ dus gsum thams cad du chags pa med pa'i sems dang ye shes kyi yul rgyas par 'gengs pa/ byang chub sems
49b8(phal chen): dpa'i yon tan dang / nan tan yongasu rdzogs pa thams cad bskal pa brjod du med par rgyun mi 'chad par 'angs par bstan pa la yon tan bsngags shing / brjod bzang mi shes pa sha stag ste/ 'di ltar byang
50a1(phal chen): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rin po che'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po pad mo'i snying
50a2(phal chen): po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po pad mo dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po nyi ma'i snying po da
50a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gtsang ba'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po zla ba dri ma med pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa'
50a4(phal chen): sems dpa' chen po rgyan rnam par dgong ba thams cad rab tu snang bar spyod pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ye shes rna ma par snang ba'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' che
50a5(phal chen): bo pal yid du 'ong ba'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po can dan dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems da pa' sems dpa' chen po me tog dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub
50a6(phal chen): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po me tog rgyas pa'i dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dpal lha'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bsod nams dpal gyi snying po dang
50a7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po baspobs pa med pa'i ye shes rnam par dag pa dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yon tan dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
50a8(phal chen): chen po mthu chen dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dri ma med pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dri ma dang bral ba'i snying po dang/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
50b1(phal chen): chen po spobs pa sna tshogs kyi rgyan gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'od zer gyi dra ba chen po rab tu snang ba'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'od dri ma med pa'i dpal gyi gzi brjid
50b2(phal chen): bzang po'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gser bzang po dri ma med pa'i dbyig gis spras pa'i gzi brjid mdzes pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mtshan thams cad kyis
50b3(phal chen): brgyan pas rnam par dag pa'i dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dpal gyi be'u rdo rje 'od 'phro bas brgyan pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'od 'bar zhing 'phro ba'i dpal
50b4(phal chen): gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po skan ma'i rgyal po 'ong rab tu snang ba'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' se mas dpa' chen po mamakha'i mdzod ye shes bsgribs pa med pa'i
50b5(phal chen): bo dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' cher po dbyangs kyi kyi la lakhor bsgribs pa med cing ngoro snyang pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gzungs kyi yod tan gyis 'gro
50b6(phal chen): ba thams cad kyi smod lam yang dag par 'dzin pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rgya mtsho'i rgyan gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab rib dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sem
50b7(phal chen): dpa' sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yon tan thams cad rnam par dag pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sangs
50b8(phal chen): rgyas dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnam par grol ba'i zla ba dang / de dag la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po tshad med pa gzhal du med pa/ grangs med pa bsam gyi
51a1(phal chen): mi khyab pa/ mtshungs pa med pa/ dpag tu med pa/ kun tu mtha' yas pa/ mu med pa/ sa 'tshams med pa/ brjod du med pa'i yang brjod med pa/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' cher po rje rje
51a2(phal chen): snying po la sogs pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing sna tshogs nas 'dus pa sha stag dang / thabs gcig tu zhugs so// de nas de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' cher po rdo rje'i snying po sangs rgyas kyi mthus theg pa chen po rab tu snga
51a3(phal chen): ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying pos/ byang chub sems dpa' ting nge 'dzin theg pa chen po rab tu snang ba de la mnyam par bzhag ma thag tu/ de nas
51a4(phal chen): de'i sa phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi phyogs re re'i 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi dbye ba phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol danas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi dbye ba phrag 'a
51a5(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kun kyang mtshar rdo rje'i snying po zhes bya bar 'dzu ba sha stag gis zhal mngon par bstan te/ sangs rgyas bcu ma ldan 'das de dag gis de la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rig
51a6(phal chen): kyi bu de ltar khyod byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin theg pa chen po rab tu snang ba la snyoms par du la zhe po legs so// 'di ltar rigs kyi bu khyod la phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba phrag
51a7(phal chen): bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kun kyang mtsham rdo rje'i snying po zhes bya bar 'thun pa sha stag gis bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad 'di'i sngor gyi spon lam
51a8(phal chen): gyi byin gyi brlabs dang / khyod nyid kyi ye shes kyi khyad par gyis/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la sangs rgyas rgya chos snang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa rab tu brjod cing / ye shes kyi sa la 'jug par bya ba dang / dge ba'i
51b1(phal chen): ba thams cad yang dag par bsdu ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad rab tu dbye ba la mkhas par bya ba dang / chos thams cad la ye shes shin tu yangs pa dub pa dang / shin tu legs par gnas pa'i chos rab tu bstan pa dang / ye shes
51b2(phal chen): tha mi dad pa rnam par spang ba dang / 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad kyis gos pa med par bya ba dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba yongasasu dag par bya ba dang / ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i yul khong du rgud par bya ba
51b3(phal chen): nas thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi yul gyi bar du khong du chud par bya ba dang / 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu brtsams pa rab tu 'thob par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sa ma nor bar rnam par dgod pa shin tu bstan pa dang / 
51b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la yang dag par dmigs par bya ba dang / zag pa med pa'i chos kyi bye brag rnam par bsgom pa dang / rnam par dbye ba shin tu rnam par phye ba'i shes rab kyi sdang ba chen po la mkhas pa'i
51b5(phal chen): ye shes kyi rgyan thob par bya ba dang / shin tu brtags pa'i ye shes kyi sgo la 'jug par bya ba dang / gnas kyi rnam pa ji rig su brjod ba dang / spobs pa'i snang pa dma' ba med par thob par bya ba dang / tha da
51b6(phal chen): pa yang dag par shes pa cher pos shin tu rtogs par bya ba dang / byang chub kyi sems la dram pa nyams pa med par bya ba dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad yong su smin par bya ba dang / thams cad du song ba'i blo rnam par gdon mi
51b7(phal chen): za ba la mkhas pa rab tu 'thob par bya ba'i phyir byin gyis brlab pa mdzad do// de bas na rigs kyi bu khyod kyis chos kyi sgo rab tu dbye ba la mkhas par 'gyur ba'i chos kyi rnab grangs 'di la sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / de bzhin gsheg
51b8(phal chen): pa'i ye shes snga ba'i byin gyis brlabs kyis rang gi dge ba'i rtsa ba yong su dag par bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings shin tu spyad pa dang / sems cad gyi khams thams cad la phan gangags pa dang / chos kyi sku'i ye shes kyi lus la
52a1(phal chen): 'jug par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyis dbang bskur ba yang dag par blang ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du shin tu 'phags pa'i lus 'byung bar bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi
52a2(phal chen): lam gyi rgyud thams cad las yang dag par 'da' bar bya ba dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyi tshul yongasu dag par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yong su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir spobs pa snyed cig/ de nas
52a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po la zil gyis mi non pa'i lus nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// thogs pa med pa'i spobs pas shin tu ston pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// shin du sbyangs pa
52a4(phal chen): ye shes rnas par phye ba la 'jug pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// dran pa nyams pa med pa'i byin gyi brlabs pa bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// zlo gros shing du nges par rtogs pas mkhas pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzang
52a5(phal chen): thams cad kyi rjesu song bar blo rjes su 'gro ba nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad// yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi stongs thub pa med pa nye bang bsgrub pa mdzad do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i mi 'jigs
52a6(phal chen): che zhing zhum pa med pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes dang dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pas rnam par dbye ba'i chos kyi tshul shin tu rtogs par bya ba nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// de bzhin gshegs pa thams
52a7(phal chen): cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rgyan shin tu rnam par phye ba mngon par bsdu ba nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni ting 'dzin de nyid kyi chos nyid rab tu thob pa dang / sngon gyi smod lam gyis mngon par bsgrubs
52a8(phal chen): ba dang / lhag pa'i bsam pa shin tu rnam par spangs pa dang / ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor shin du sbyangs pa dang / tshogs shin tu bsags pa dang / yongasu sbyangs pa shin tu byas pa dang / dran pa'i sdong tshad med/ 
52b1(phal chen): pa dang / mos pa rnam par dag cing 'ong shin tu gsal ba dang / gzungs kyi sgo tha dad pa med par thob pa dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi ye shes kyi phyag rgyas shin tu btab pa'i phyir ro// de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis de
52b2(phal chen): ngag ma zhugs bzhin du rdzu 'phrul gyi mthus so so nas phyag g.yas pa brkyang te/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po'i mgo la byug pa mdzad do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis/ byang chub sems dpa'
52b3(phal chen): rdo rje'i snying po la reg ma thag tu de nyid kyi tshe/ ting nge 'dzin de las langs nas/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag la spras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ byang chub sems dpa'i smong lam shin tu rnam par gdod mi za ba ste/ tha mi
52b4(phal chen): dang pa balngar med pa chos kyi dbyings kyis klas par yangs pa nam ma pa'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa'i phyi ma'i mtha'i ngur thug pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad rgyas
52b5(phal chen): par khyab pa/ 'gro ba thams cad yongasu skyob pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byin gyi brlabs pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras da gangs ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ram
52b6(phal chen): 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi ye shes kyi sa la yang rab tu 'jug par 'gyur ro// ma pyod pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ye shes kyi sa la yang rab tu 'jug par 'gyur ro// da ltar byung ba'i sa
52b7(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ye shes kyi sa la yang rab tu 'jug par 'gyur ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes kyis rnams te/ gang la bsam te bdag gis
52b8(phal chen): de skad du smras pa de dag ni 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / nga ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis gsungs so// gsung ngo // gsung bar 'gyur ro// bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ rab tu dga' ba che
53a1(phal chen): bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i sadang po dang / dri ma dang bral ba zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i sa gnyis pa dang / 'od byed pa zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa gsum pa dang / 'od 'phro bcar zhes
53a2(phal chen): bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa bzhi pa dang / rgyal bar dka' ba zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa lnga pa dang / mngon sum zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa drug pa dang / ring du song ba zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems da
53a3(phal chen): sa bdun pa dang / mi g.yo ba zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa brgyad pa dang / legs pa'i blo gros shes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa dgu pa dang / chos kyi sprid ces bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu pa ste
53a4(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag de rnams ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu ste/ de ni 'das pa dang / ma byon pa/ dang // da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis
53a5(phal chen): gsung so// gsung ngo // gsung bar 'gyur ro// kye rgyal ba'i/ sras dag bdag gis ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing na'ang de bzhin gshesas pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams
53a6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu po 'di dag mi gsung ba de lta bu ma mthong ngo // de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i lam yongasu spyod pa
53a7(phal chen): chos snang ba'i sgo 'di ni yang dag phul zhe bya ba yin te/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i sa rnam par dgod pa shin tu bstan pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag gnas 'di ni bsam gyi mi khyab pa ste/ 'di ltar byang chub sems
53a8(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyis shes pa'o// de nas de ltar byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu po 'di dag ming tsam zhig brjod de/ cang mi zer bar 'dug nas de las rab tu phye ste ma bshad pa dang / 
53b1(phal chen): de nas byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor de dag thams cad byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu po de dag gi ming tsam zhig thos nas rab tu phye ste ma brjod pas skom par gyur nas/ de dag 'di snyam du sems te/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa'
53b2(phal chen): rdo rje'i snying pos byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu po de dag gi ming tsam zhig brjod de cang mi zer bar 'dug na de las rab tu phye zhing pi stor pa de la rgyu ni gang rkyen ni ci zhig yod snyam pa dang / de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' 'khor 'dus
53b3(phal chen): bden/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnam par grol ba'i zla ba zhes bya ba 'dus shing / 'dug 'dug sde/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' rnam par grol ba'i zla bas byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor de dag gi sems
53b4(phal chen): kyis yongasu shes nas/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po la klu'i dbyangs kyis tshigs su bcad de dor de dris/ ci phyir rtog pa rnam dag cing // dran dang ye shes ldan pa yis// sa'i mchog ni brjod byas
53b5(phal chen): mkhas pas rnam par khyi mi bshad// 'di kun nges parartogs pa ste// byang chub sems dpa' grags chen ming / ci phyir khyod ris brjod de// rab tu phye ba bshad mi bgyi/ rgyal
53b6(phal chen): sras 'jigs med 'di dag ni// kun kyang shin tu 'an par 'dod// sde tshul yang dag tu// rnam par phye ste bshad pa mdzod// 'khor 'di shin tu rnam dang ste// le lo med cing dge dang ldan/ dag pa'i mchog
53b7(phal chen): la gnas pa ste/ yon tan ye shes ldan pa yin// phan tshun gcig la gcig lta zhing // kun kyang rim gro bcas par gnas// sbrang rtsi ji ltar spang min pa// de ltar bdud rtsi mchog kyang 'dod// rdo rje'i snying po
53b8(phal chen): 'jigs med pa// shes rab chen pos de thos nas/ 'khor rnams dga' bar bya ba'i phyir// bde bar gshegs pa'i sras la smras// sangs rgyas sku rab yang dag 'byung bas na// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa
54a1(phal chen): rab bstan cing // sargyungs pa rnam par dbye bya ba// de'i rmang byung mchog tu dga' ba yid// pra zhing blta dka' sa par rtog pa sdangs// sems kyis dang bral bas bsgrub par dga'// mtha
54a2(phal chen): ba rnams kyi zag med spyod yul te// 'gro ba rnams kyis de bos mos par 'gyur// rdo rje lta bung bsas pa rab bzhag ste/ sangs rgyas ye shes mchog la mos byas shing // bdag med pa'i sems kyis shes ra// ye
54a3(phal chen): shes ngas pa 'di gzod mnyan par nus// ji ltar bar snang tshon ris bri ba dang / namakha'i dbyings la rlung gnas ji bzhin du/ de ltar ye shes zag pa med pa yang // shin tu lha dka' thub pas rnam par phye// de la bdag gi
54a4(phal chen): sems ni 'di snyam byed// sangs rgyas ye shes dam pa bsam yas la// 'gro ba gang rnams dang par byed dkon zhes/ de'i phyir nam smras ma bshad do// de skad ces smras pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'
54a5(phal chen): rnam par grol ba'i zla bas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po la/ 'di skad ces smras so// kye rgyal ba'i sras 'khor 'di ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos 'di dag la
54a6(phal chen): bsam pa shin tu sbyangs pa/ kun tu rtog pa yongasu spangs pa/ spyad par bya ba shin tu spyad pa/ tshogs shin tu bsags pa/ sangs rgyas kyi ba khrag khrig brgya stong shin tu bsnyen bkur ba/ yon tan dang ye shes
54a7(phal chen): tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ the tsom dang nem nur med pa nyodan mongs pa dang bral ba mos pa dang lhag pa'i bsam pa la rab tu gnas pa/ gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog sha stag tshogs pas yong su dag pa yin gyis/ kye rgyal
54a8(phal chen): ba'i sras de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis legs par bshad ba mdzod cig dang / byang chub sems dpa' 'di dag thams cad mi rnam pa 'di lta bu'i gnas zang mo la mngon sum du gnas pa sha stag go// de nas byang chub
54b1(phal chen): sems dpa' rnam par grol ba'i zla bas ngom 'di nyid gsar bar bzlas pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bla med pa/ sa rnams rab phye rnam dgod brtag
54b2(phal chen): pa yi// ye shes sbyong zhing byang chub 'thob byed pa// mchog dang dam pa bzhi pa'i chos rnams shod// 'khor ni dag pa nyon mongs med pa'i mchog/ mos dang bsam pa shin tu spangs pa ste/ sangs rgyas bye ba mang la spyad pa
54b3(phal chen): spang // sa 'di brtag la yid ches ldan pa yin// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos byang chub sems dpa' rnam par grol ba'i zla ba la 'di skad ces smras so// kye rgyal ba'i sras 'khor 'di ltar byang chub sems
54b4(phal chen): dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos kyi rnam pa 'di lta bu'i gnas zab mo la bsam pa shin tu spangs pa/ kun tu rtogs pa yongasu spangs pa/ spyad pa shin du spyad pa/ tshogs shin tu bsags pa/ sangs
54b5(phal chen): rgyas bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong la dge ba'i rtsa ba shin tu bsags pa/ yon tan dang ye shes tshad med pa dang ldan pa the tshom dang nem nur med pa/ nyon mongs pa dang bral ba/ mos pa dang
54b6(phal chen): lhag pa'i bsam pa la rab tu gnas pa gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa sha stag tshogs pas shin tu dag pa yang yin na/ 'on kyang sems can ngos pa chung ngu gzhan dag gis zab mo'i rnam pa 'di lta bu bsam gyi mi khyab
54b7(phal chen): pa'i gnas dag thos par gyur la/ thos nas kyang the tshom dang yid gnyis su gyur na/ de dag la yun ring por gnod pa dang / don med pa dang / mi bde ba'i rgyur 'gyur bas/ 'di lta zhig du snying brtse ba'i phyir/ bdag
54b8(phal chen): mi cang mi zer bar 'dug pa nyid du mos so// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos ngon 'di nyid gsal bar bsum pa'i phyir tshigs su bcad pa 'ang dag smras so// 'khor 'di rnam ngag shes rab yangs paste
55a1(phal chen): rab ci gsal ba'i spyod lngan tshogs shes shing // gzhan dring mi 'jog rgyal ba'i nga mi g.yo// bsam chog mi 'jug rgya mtsho chen po dra/ 'od kyang mtshogs mi shes pa smyung ba// rnam shes su
55a2(phal chen): gnas don la shes med pas// thos shing mches 'phral du ngan song lhung // de dag snying brtses ye shes sam bshad// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rnam par grol ba'i zla bas yang / byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po la gsol ba
55a3(phal chen): btab pa/ rgyal ba'i sras legs par bshad par rjod cig dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis rnam pa 'di lta bu bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gnas 'di dag kyang gzhan du mi 'gyur ba dang / legs par yid ches par 'gyur ro// 
55a4(phal chen): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras don 'di ltar sa 'di shin tu bsnam pa 'di bshad pa'i tshechos nyid rab tu thob pas/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis kyang dgongs par 'gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyang ye
55a5(phal chen): shes kyis 'di yong su bsrung ba'i don du rab tu brtsom par byed do// de yang zud phyir zhes/ 'dir spong ba'i sa dang po ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yang dag par 'grub pa'i gzhi yin no// kye rgyal
55a6(phal chen): ba'i sras 'di lta ste/ dpeng nga ye ge dang bru 'grangs ba 'i snyed du ste na bde dag thams cad kyi sngod du 'gro ba'ang mig bya ma'o// bamar yang meg phyi mo la 'dug ste/ yiga'i phyi mo bsnyud pas ma khyab pa de lu bu'i rige
55a7(phal chen): 'bru 'grangs pa bstan pa ni gang yang mang ngo // kye rgyal ba'i sras de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyang spyod pas rab tu 'grub pas sa sngon du 'gro'o// rang byung gi ye shes kyi mthar thug par 'gyur bas sa'i mthar thug pa'o//

55b1(phal chen): zla bas ngor 'di nyid gsal bar bzlas pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po la tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ sa dang spyod 'jug byang chub 'gyur ba ye shes smra byed pa// spyod pa rnam dag thams cad mkhyen pa'i sras kyi legs par
55b2(phal chen): sho / phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba bde gshegs kur mgon 'dren pa ji snyed pa// khyu mchog de kun ye shes 'byung gnas ston la dgongs pa mdzad// 'di mi dang po zhugs pa'i shes spyod 'di yi mthar thug ste/ rgyal ba'i chos rab gzhal yas
55b3(phal chen): ji snyed de dag 'byung gnas 'di// yi ge 'brangs pa'i phyi mo'i rjes 'gro sngon du de 'gro ltar/ de bzhin sa mchog blo'i yul du tha ma thug par 'dong // de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyis dbyangs kyi nga ro gcig tu glu'i bya
55b4(phal chen): kyis tshigs su bcad de/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po la ngon 'di nyid kyi phyir/ gsol ba btab pa/ blo yangs dpa pa'i phul ma nga' ba// stobs pa mtha' yas rnam par dbye ba rtogs mkhyen pas/ 
55b5(phal chen): yid du 'ong ba'i gsung dbyangs kyis// kun la pha dog ngas pa bshad pa mdzod// drang dang dga' bas spyod dag pa// stobs bcu'i stong sa kyi shugs spogs yon tad ldan pa yi/ sa yi ngas pa mchog
