56a1(phal chen): bya ba'i 'od zer 'khor gyi 'od zer brgya stong grangs med pa dang ldan pa byung ngo // de byung nas phyogs bcu thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus par snang bar byas nas/ sems cad
56a2(phal chen): thams cad kyi ngan song gi sdug bsngal thams cad rtsel bar byas te/ bdud kyi khyim thams cad zil gyis marang nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor snang bar byas te/ sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi rnam pa bsam
56a3(phal chen): gyi mi khyab pa'i mthu bstan nas/ phyogs bcu thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du chos bstan pa'i byid gyi brlabs kyis byin du brlabs pa'i
56a4(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i lus snang bar byas/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam pa 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa bstan nas/ steng gi bar snang la 'od zer stug po'i sprid gyi dra ba'i khang pa brtsegs pa chen por byas ste 'dug
56a5(phal chen): go// de bzhin du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gi mdzod spu ngag nas kyang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'ong snang ba zhes bya ba'i 'od zer 'khor gyi 'od zer grangs med pa dang ldan pa dag byung bar gyur
56a6(phal chen): to/ byung nas kyang de dag gis phyogs bcu thams cad du 'jig rted gyi khams 'byas klas pa kun tu de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil labe ra du chos bstan pa'i byin gyis byin du brlabs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
56a7(phal chen): rnabs snang bar byas te/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa bstan nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed 'di yang snang bar byas/ bcom ldan 'das shA kya thub pa de bzhir gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi
56a8(phal chen): dkyil 'khor 'di yang snang bar byas te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po'i lus kyang snang bar byas na/ steng gi bar snang la de bzhin du 'od zer stug po'i sprir gyi dra ba'i khang pa brtsegs pa
56b1(phal chen): chen por byas te 'khod do// de nas 'od zer stug po'i spring gyi dra ba'i khang pa brtsegs pa chen po ngag na sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis sgra'i rnam pa 'di lta bu 'di byung ngo // mi mnyam mnyam dang mnyam pa mkha' dang mnyam pa dag/ stobs bcu'i
56b2(phal chen): khyu mchog mthu ldan tshad med yon tan can/ 'jig rten ku chog ma'i dam pa phul gyi rnabs// shAkya seng ge'i chos la byin rlabs dam pa mdzad/ bde gshegs sras po 'dren pa'i byin gyis bshad par gyis// chos rgyal khyu
56b3(phal chen): mchog rnams kyi mdzod kyi dam pa phye// sa'i ye shes rnam phye spyod mchog rab yangs pa// stobs bcu'i byin gyis ma thogs myur du bstan pa gyis// gang gis rna lam bsam par chos dam rin chen 'di// song bar gyur pa de dag
56b4(phal chen): bde gshegs byin gyis brlabs// rdul mengs kun rim gyis rab tu rdzogs byas nas// stobs bcu ldan pa'i rgyal ba dam par 'grub par 'gyur/ rgya mtsho'i chu byung gyur cing bskal pa'i mes gdungs kyang
56b5(phal chen): gal te snod gyur sems can de dag 'di la nyan// gang rnams the chom tha zhing yid gnyis byed pa ni// de dag rdzabs rnam pa kun tu thos mi 'gyur// de phyir sa'i ye shes lam mchog bstan par gyis/ 
56b6(phal chen): gnas dang rgyud dang 'phro ba rim gyis rab tu shong // spyod dang yul dang chos dang ye shes tshul rnams kyi// chos kyi tshul yang 'gro ba kun la phan phyir shod// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos phyogs bcur bltas
56b7(phal chen): nas 'khor thams cad de bas kyang dad par bya ba'i phyir/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcang ba 'di dag smras so// phral shes dka' drang srong chen po'i lam/ mi rtog rtog yul ma yin blta bar dka'// rang bzhin ni zhing 'gag
56b8(phal chen): med 'byung ba med// mkhas gsal shes pas khong du chud pa yid// ngo bo nyid stong zhi zhing sdug bsngal zad // rgyud las rnam grol mnyam par mya ngan 'das// mtha' dang dpung med tshig gis brjod du med// dus gsum grol
57a1(phal chen): ba na mnga' 'dra zhing mtshungs// bde gshegs spyod yul zhi zhing nye bar zhi// smra ba'i lam rnams kun gyis brjod par dga'// de dag sa dang spyod pa de 'dra bas// smra bar dka' na bstan par ga la nus
57a2(phal chen): de ni bsam yas sems lam rnam par spangs// ye shes mngon bsgrubs rgyal ba'i spyod yul te// phung po skye mched khams kyis bskyed pa min// sems kyis mi shes yid kyis rnam ma rtags// ji ltar bar snang gnas kyi bya'i rjes/ 
57a3(phal chen): shin tu sma dka' bstan par mi nus pa// re ltar bde gshegs sras kyi sa rnams kyang // yid dang sems kyi yul gyis shes mi nus/ 'on kyang byams dang snying rje'i smod lam gyis// de las phyogs tsam rim pa'i tshul ba'i du/ 
57a4(phal chen): bshad par bya ste sems kyi spyod yul mim/ ye shes tshul gyis rdzogs par bya'o// de 'dra'i spyod yul phra zhing blta dka' ba// rang rig yin bas brjod par ma rus kyang // 'od kyang bde bar gshegs pa'i mthus
57a5(phal chen): gor kyis// thams cad 'thun par nan tan gyis te nyod// ye na sas dang spyod 'jug ci 'dra ba// bskal 'bye bar zang par mi nus te/ yang dag ngor dngos gzhan min gnas pa las/ mdo tsam bshad
57a6(phal chen): kyis de dag mnyam par gyis// 'thum zhing nan tan yod par sta gon gnos// bde gshegs byin gyis bdag gis bshad par bya// dpe ldan 'thang la yi ge mnyam pa yi// chos sbyangs pa bdag gis brjod par bya// 'di ni tshig
57a7(phal chen): gis brjod par shin tu dka'// de ltar tshad med bde gshegs mthu ngag las// chu thigs gcig 'dra bdag gi lus 'di la// de ring zhugs kyis bshad pa mnyan par gyis// kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag de la sems can dge ba'i rtsa
57a8(phal chen): ba shin tu bsags pa sbyang ba shin du spyad pa/ tshogs shin tu bsags pa/ sangs rgyas byung ba shin tu bsnyen bkur ba/ chos dkar po shin tu bsdus pa/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis shin tu bzung ba bsam pa yong su dag pa/ lhag pa
57b1(phal chen): bsam pa shin tu rgya chen po can pos pa rgya chen po dang ldan pa/ snying rje dang snying brtse ba mngon du gyur pa/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes la mngon par mos pa rnams/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la mos pa dang / stobs bcu'i stobs
57b2(phal chen): thob par bya ba dang / mi 'jigs pa chen po thob par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi tshogs mnyam pa nyid thob par bya dang / 'gro ba thams cad yongasu bskyab par bya ba dang / snying brtse ba dang snying rje chen po yong su dag par bya ba dang / phyogs
57b3(phal chen): bcu ma lus par thogs pa med pa'i ye shes mngon du 'gyur bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing ma lus pa thams cad thogs pa med par yongasu sbyang bar bya ba dang / dus gsum thams cad skad cig gcig gis khong du chud par bya
57b4(phal chen): ba dang chos kyi 'khor lo chen po rab tu bskor ba la khyu mchog gi mthu dbyung ba rgya chen po 'thob par bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems snying rje chen po sngon du 'gro ba/ shes rab dang / ye
57b5(phal chen): shes kyi dbang du gyur pa/ thabs mkhas pas yong su bzung ba/ sam pa dang lhag pa'i bsam pas rab tu bsdam pa/ de bzhin / gshegs pa'i stobs tshang med pa dang ldan pa/ sems can
57b6(phal chen): gyi spobs dang / blo'i spongs rnam par dbye bar bya ba/ shin tu rnam par phye ba/ chags pa med pa'i ye shes mngon tu gyur pa/ rang byung gi ye shes dang / 'thur ba sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos la shes rab dang
57b7(phal chen): ye shes kyi mam sa yang dag pa dzalu Ta/ sangs rgyas byung ba thams cad las gdams ngag yang dag par smras pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyis rmas pa dang / mam kha'i mthar thug par gnas pa/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa
57b8(phal chen): sme bar 'gyur te/ sems bskyed pa de bskyed par gra hA byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po so so'i skye bo'i sa las rab tu 'das pa yin// byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med pa shin tu nom pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs
58a1(phal chen): nga'i rigs su skyes pa yin/ rigs brjong pa la kham ma po 'i beng ba yid/ 'jig ched gyi kha thams cad las phyir log pa mi/ 'jig ched las 'das pa'i las shing tu dong pa yid/ byang dub se
58a2(phal chen): dpa'i chos nyid la gnas pa yin// byang chub sems dpa'i rngam par dgod pa la rab tu gnas pa yin/ dus gsum mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su song ba yin/ rdzogs pa'i byang chub la shing tu gzhol bas de bzhin gshegs pa'i ris
58a3(phal chen): su nges pa yid/ kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag chos kyi rab pa 'di lta bu la gnas pa yid/ byang dub sems dpa' ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa rab tu dga' ba la mi g.yo ba'i tshul gyis rab tu gangs so// kye rgyal ba'i sras
58a4(phal chen): ngag de la byang chub sems dpa'i sa rab tu dga' ba la gnas pa'i bya rkub sems dpa' ni rab tu dga' ba bang ba yin/ yid bde ba mang ba yin/ bos pa mang ba yin/ rangs pa mang ba yin/ mgu
58a5(phal chen): ba mang ba yin/ spro ba mang ba yin/ 'tshe ba med pa mang ba yin/ khro ba med pa mang ba yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de ltar byang du/ ba sems dpa'i sa rab tu dga' ba la gdas pa'i byang chub sems
58a6(phal chen): dpa' ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dpas rjesu drang zhing rab tu dga' ba yid/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams rjesu drang zhing rab tu dga' ba yin/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' cher po rnams rjesu drang 'ang rab tu
58a7(phal chen): dga' ba yin/ byang chub sems dpa'i spong ba drang zhing rab tu dga' ba yin/ pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par dag pa rjes dran zhing rab tu dga' ba yid/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa'i khyad par rjesu drang zhing rab tu dga'
58a8(phal chen): ba yid/ byang chub mings dpa'i spyo su mi 'drogs gsu drang ning ba tu dga' ba mim pa de bzhing gshegs pa'i bdabs papa dang / rgya chu drang zhing rab tu ga' ba yin / sems cad gyi ngo ma
58b1(phal chen): thob par bya ba rje su drar zhing rab tu dga' ba yid/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes la 'jug pa'i thabs rje su drang zhing rab tu dga' ba yin/ yang de 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag ni 'gro ba thams cad kyi yul las
58b2(phal chen): phyir log go zhes rab tu dga' ba bskyed do// bdag ni sangs rgyas kyi sa dang nye bar gyur to zhes rab tu dga' ba skyed // bdag ni byis pa'i sa las ring du gyur to zhes rab tu dga' bskyed do// bdag ri ye shes kyis dang nye bar
58b3(phal chen): gyur ro zhes rab tu dga' ba skyed do// bdag ni ngan song dang ngaran 'gro'o 'jigs pa thams cad rgyun chang ngo // zhes rab tu dga' ba skyed do// bdag ni sems can thams cad kyi gnas su gyur to zhes rab tu dga' ba skyed do// 
58b4(phal chen): bdag gis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad bathob par 'gyur ba dang / nye bar gyur to zhes rab tu dga' ba skyed do// bdag ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul la yang dag par byung ngo // zhes rab tu dga'
58b5(phal chen): bsred do// bdag ni byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi mnya/ pa nyid dang ldan par gyur to zhes rab tu dga' bskyed do// bang / ga ni 'jigs pa dang / bag tsha ba dang / sdang ba dang /

58b7(phal chen): 'jigs pa'i rnam pa 'di dag 'di lta ste/ 'tshe ba med pas 'jigs pa 'am/ mi bsngags pas 'jigs pa 'am/ 'chi bas 'jigs pa 'as/ ngar song gi 'jigs pa 'am/ 'khor du bag tsha bas 'jigs pa de dag thams
58b8(phal chen): cang de la med pa yin/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de ni bdag gi 'du shes dang bral bas/ de la bdag phangs par sems pa'ang med na/ yo byad thams cad la phangs par sems pa lta ga la yod de/ de'i phyir nge
59a1(phal chen): 'jo pa lags pa med do// ngan sulas pa sa thong kya cu cams me du lags du pa ga kyi sems cad dag la 'ang ba pa sa nga ga/ 
59a2(phal chen): sems dpas de'i phyir de la mi bsngags pa'i 'jigs pa med do// de bdag tu lta ba dang 'bral bas de la bdag gi 'du shes med de/ de'i phyir de la 'chi ba'i 'jigs pa med do// ngag shinas kyang 'don mi za bar/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub
59a3(phal chen): sems dpa' dag dang mi 'bral bar 'gyur ro zhes de'i phyir de la ngan song gi 'jigs pa med do// de 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gi bsam pa dang / 'jig rten na mtshungs pa'ang su yang med na lhag pa lta ga la yod ces de'i phyir de la 'a'o//

59a6(phal chen): rtog pa mang ba dang / snying rtse ba dang / snying rjes mngon par sgrub pa dang / byams pa chen po dang ldan pa dang / yid spro ba med pa dang / ngo tsha shes pa dang / khrel yod ba'i rgyan dang / bzod cing nges pa dang ldan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs/

59b3(phal chen): ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs la skyon du 'gyur bar mi byed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i bslab pa mi gtong ba dang / ri'i dbang po'i rgyal po chen po ltar thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems mi tshul ba dang / 'jig rten gyi bya ba
59b4(phal chen): thams cad la mngon par dga' ba med pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'i lam dang ldan pa dang / mi ngoms par byang chub kyi yan lag gi tshogs rab tu bsags pa dang / rtag tu rgyur mi chad
59b5(phal chen): par gong nas gong du khyad par 'bogs pa'i lam tshol ba dang / sa yod su sbyong ba'i chos kyi rnam pa 'di lta bu dag dang ldan pa'i byang chub semasadapa' sems dpa' chen po mi/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa rab tu dga'
59b6(phal chen): bal gnas pa yin te/ de byang chub sems dpa'i sa rab tu dga' ba de la shin tu gnas shing / rnam pa 'di lta bu'i smod lam chen po dang / brtson pa chen po dang / mngon par bsgrub pa chen po 'di dag mngon par sgrub ste/ 'di ltar sangs
59b7(phal chen): rgyas thams cad ma lus pa lhag ma med pa mtha' dag la mchod cing ring gro bya ba'i phyir/ rnam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa mos pa rgya chen pos rnam par dag pa chos kyi dbyings kyis klas par rgya che ba/ namakha'i dbyings
59b8(phal chen): kyi bar thug pa/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa bskal pa 'grangs pa thams cad du sangs rgyas skye ba 'grangs pa la rim gro dang / mchod pa cher po bya ba rgyun mi chad pa'i sngor lam chen po mngor bar sgrub po// 'di lta ste/ de bzhin
60a1(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsungs pa'i chos kyi tshul yang dag par bzung ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub yang dag par blang ba dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bskrad pa

60a7(phal chen): du sangs rgyas 'byung ba 'grangs pa'i drung du 'gro ba nas/ mya ngan las 'das pa chen po'i bar gyi drung du 'gro ba rgyun mi 'chang ba'i smod lam chen po mngon par sgrub po// 'di lta ste byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya chen po shin tu yangs

60b1(phal chen): nyid du bcas pa dang / 'grub pa dang / 'jig pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod par gtogs pa thams cad dang sa ji lta ba bzhin dang / ji lta bur bstan pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa yongasu sbyang ba la gdangs ngag dang / man ngag sbyin pas

61a1(phal chen): phyogs bcu'i rnam pa tha dad par lus pa'i drang pa la 'jug pa rnam par phye ba'i ye shes khong du chud cing / mngon du 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings kyis klas par rgya che ba nang kha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa

61a3(phal chen): cang zhing gcig tu yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba dang / zhing gcig zhing thams cad du yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba dang / yongasu sbyang ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing tshang pa 'od mang po'i rgyan gyis rab tu brgyan par bya ba dang / kun nas nyon

61a8(phal chen): sangs rgyas 'byung ba ci dgar bstan pa dang / rang gi sems bskyed pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul dang mthu dang / ye shes khong du chud par bya ba dang / ma nyams shing rje su 'brang ba'i mngon par shes pa rab tu thob par
61b1(phal chen): bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rnam par rgyu bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'khor du gzugs brnyan 'byung ba yang dag par bstan pa dang / skye ba'i skye gnas thams cad du rang gi lus rje su 'gro bar bya ba dang / theg pa
61b2(phal chen): chen po bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad spyad pa rgyun mi 'chad pa'i phyir/ chos kyi dbyings kyis klas par rgya che ba na mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa'i phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa/ bskal pa 'grangs
61b3(phal chen): pa thams cad du spyod pa 'grangs par theg pa chen po mngon par bsgrub pa la/ rgyun mi 'chad pa'i smon lam chen po mngon par sgrub po// 'di lta ste phyir mi ldog pa'i 'khor lo la yang dag par gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod
61b4(phal chen): baspyad pa dang / lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las don yod par bya ba dang / mthong ma thag tu sangs rgyas kyi chos gdon ma za bar 'thob par bya ba dang / dbyangs brjod ma thag tu ye shes khong du chud par bya ba dang / dang bar
61b5(phal chen): gyur ma thag tu nyon mongs pa phyir mi ldog par bya ba dang / bsam pa sman gyi rgyal po chen po lta bu rab tu thob par bya ba dang / lus yid bzhin gyi nor bu lta bu 'thob par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' spyod
61b6(phal chen): pa thams cad spyad pa'i phyir chos kyi dbyings kyis klas par rgya che ba mamakha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa phyi ma'i mtha' mur thug pa/ bskal pa 'grangs pa thams cad du phyir mi ldog pa'i 'khor lo 'grangs par spyod pa thams cad 'bras bu

61b8(phal chen): sgra'i sbubs thams cad du tshe dang / skye ba dang / ge zhon nu rol pa dang / btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang na bzhugs pa dang / mngon par 'byung ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa dang / snying po byang chub tu gshegs pa dang / bdud
62a1(phal chen): gdul ba dang / mngon par 'tshang rgya ba dang / gsol pa gdab pa dang / chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba chen po bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi yul dang mthu dang / ye shes
62a2(phal chen): chen po khong du chud par bya ba dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du sangs rgyas 'byung ba dang skad cig skad cig tu mngon par 'tshang rgya ba dang / rab tu zhi ba thob par bya ba yang dag par bstan pa dang / mngon
62a3(phal chen): bar 'tshang rgya ba gcig gis chos kyi dbyings thams cad 'phrul pas rgyas par dgang ba dang / dbyangs gcig brjod pas sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi sems dang / bsam pa shin tu tshim par bya ba dang / mya ngan las 'das pa chen
62a4(phal chen): po yongs su bstan pa dang / spyod pa rnams rgyud mi 'chang ba ra bya ba dang / theg pa chen po'i sa la chos thams cad rnam par dgod pa yang dag par bstan pa dang / chos shes pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi sgyu dang mngon par shes

63a1(phal chen): ces/ de ltar sngon lam shin tu bsgrubs shing / phan pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ lam pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ las su rung ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ zhi ba'i sems dang ldan pa// dul ba'i sems dang ldan pa

63a3(phal chen): gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi sngon gyi mtha'i spyod pa mngon par bsgrubs pa'i rgyud la yid ches pa yin/ pha rol tu phyin pa yang dag par bsdu ba la yid ches pa yin/ sa yang dag par bsgrub pa dang / 
63a4(phal chen): khyad par du 'gyur ba la mngon par yid ches pa yin/ stobs yod su 'grub pa la mngon par yid ches pa yin/ mi 'jigs pa yong su rdzogs par 'gyur ba la mngon par yid ches pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa

63b1(phal chen): skye bo 'di dag lta ba ngan par lhung ba'i rgyud dang / ma rig pa'i mun nag dang / rab rib kyi thibs pos kun nas khebs pa'i yid dang nga rgyal gyi rgyal gyi rgyal mtshan shin tu bsgreng ba'i yongasu rtog pa dang / sred pa'i dra bas mngon par ye

66b1(phal chen): pa yin te/ lam gyi bar lam de nas ma 'phags par de nyid nas shes pas shin tu brtags pa'i blo dang / brgyags kyi tshogs chen po phun sum tshogs pas las grogs mang po rnams nyam nyes med par grong rdal cher po dang phyin par byed
66b2(phal chen): de/ mya ngan dang dgon pa'i nyes pas bdag dang lam grogs rnams la gnod par mi 'gyur bar byed do// kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag de bzhin du/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dang dpon mkhas pa yang gang gi tshe/ byang chub
66b3(phal chen): sems dpa'i sa dang po la gnas shing / sa phyogs dang / mi mthun pa'i phyogs la mkhas pa dang / sa 'grub pa dang / 'jigs pa la mkhas pha dang / sa'i rnam pa dang / rgyu 'thun pa'i 'bras bu la mkhas pa dang
66b4(phal chen): sa 'thob par bya ba dang / rnam par bsgom pa la mkhas pa dang / sa'i yan lag yongasu spangs pa la mkhas pa dang / sa nas sar 'phar ba la mkhas pa dang // sa nas sar rnam par gnas pa la mkhas pa dang
66b5(phal chen): sanas sar khyad par du 'gyur ba'i ye shes la mkhas pa dang / sa nas sa thob pa las phyir mi ldog pa la mkhas pa dang / byang chub se mas dpa'i sa thams cad yongasu spyod pas de ba'in gshegs
66b6(phal chen): pa'i sa gnon pa la mkhas par gyur pa de'i tshe bsod nams kyi tshogs chen po'i brgyags yongs su gzung ba dang / ye shes kyi tshogs chen po la rnam par dbye ba shin tu byas pa dang / sems can gyi lam grogs mang po yongs su
66b7(phal chen): gdon ba'i bsam pa dang ldan pas thams cad mkhyen pa'i grong rdal chen por phyin par bya bar 'dod cing thog ma nas sa'i lam dang / sa'i lam gyi yon tan dang / sa'i lam gol ba'i nyes pa dang / sa'i lam gyi bar lam gyi khyad par
66b8(phal chen): dang / sa'i lam gyi bar lam 'khrul mnyes par 'gyur ba dang / bsod nams kyi tshogs chen po'i brgyags pashams shing bsogs pa dag kyang / sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' ngag dang / dge ba'i gshes
67a1(phal chen): gnyen dag las yongasu tshol zhing yongasu 'dri ste// de lam gyi bar lam dang po nas gyerd du'angags par thams cad mkhyen pa'i grong rdal chen por phyin par bya ba'i bar du mkhas pa yin/ de de ltar
67a2(phal chen): ye shes kyis rnam par rdzogs pa'i blo dang / bsod dpas dang / ye shes kyi tshogs chen po'i brgyags phun sum tshogs pas/ sems can gyi lam grogs kyi tshogs chen po yongasu smin pa'i tshul bzhin du/ 'khor ba'i mya ngan dang / dgod pa
67a3(phal chen): rgal dka' ba las bsgral te/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i legs kyi grong rdal chen po'i bar du phyin par byed cing / 'khor ba'i mya ngan dang / dgon pa'i nyes pas sems can lam grogs sam/ bdag la gnod par yang mi 'gyur bar byed do// 
67a4(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bas na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos/ yongasu skyo ba med pa'i yid kyis/ sa yongasu spyad pa'i khyad par la brtso na bar bya'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi sa
67a5(phal chen): gnan pa'i bar du yang mangs par bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi byang chub sems pa'i sa dang po rab tu dga' ba'i spor 'jug pa mdor bsdus te
67a6(phal chen): bstan pa'o// rgya cher mi shi tu bstan pa brgya stong grangs med pa la rnam pa'i mur thug pa med pa ste/ bskal pa grangs med pa'i mthar thug par shin tu bstan pa'i tshul gyi khong du chud par bya'o// de la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
67a7(phal chen): sems dpa' chen po ni phal cher 'dzam+bu'i gling gi rgyal por 'gyur te/ srid chen po la dbang sgyur ba rab tu thob cing chos kyis yongasu bskyang ba dang / sems can rnams sbyin pa chen pos yongasu bsdu ba la mkhas shing mthu yod pa yin/ 
67a8(phal chen): sems can rnams kyi 'jungs pa'i dri ma bzlog pa la mkhas pa yin/ sbyin pa chen po rtsom pas yongasu dub par mi 'gyur ba yin/ de sbyin pa 'am/ ngag snyan pa 'am/ don bsgrub pa 'am/ ngon 'thun pas/ dge ba'i rtsa ba gang ji
67b1(phal chen): rtsom yang rung ste/ de thams cad ji ltar na sems can thams cad kyi mchog tu 'gyur/ gtso bor 'gyur/ thu bor 'gyur/ phul du 'gyur/ dam par 'gyur/ bla na med par 'gyur/ dren par 'gyur/ rnam par 'dren par 'gyur/ yong su 'dren
67b2(phal chen): par 'gyur ba nas thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la rten pa'i bar du 'gyur snyam ste/ sangs rgyas yid la bya ba dang / chos yid la bya ba dang / dge 'dun yid la bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' yid la bya ba dang / byang chub sems
67b3(phal chen): dpa'i spyod pa yid la bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sa yid la bya ba dang / pha rol tu phyin pa yid la bya ba dang / stobs yid la bya ba dang / mi 'jigs pa yid la bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa yid la bya ba nas/ rnam pa'i mchog
67b4(phal chen): thams cad dang ldan pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi bar du yid la bya ba dang mi 'bral ba yin/ de 'dod na skad cig yud tsam thang cig tu khyim dang chung ma dang / srid thams cad yongasu spangs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i
67b5(phal chen): bstan pa la rab tu 'byung ba dang / rab tu byung nas kyang skad cig yud tsam tha cig tu ting nge 'dzin brgya rab tu 'thob cing stobs par 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas brgya mthong ba dang / de dag gi byir gyis brlabs
67b6(phal chen): kyang yang dag par shes pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams brgya bskyod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgyar 'gro ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams brgya snang bar bya ba dang / sems can brgya yong su smin par bya ba dang / bskal pa brgyar gnas
67b7(phal chen): par bya ba dang / sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa brgya la rab tu 'jug pa dang / chos kyi sgo brgya rnam par 'byed pa dang / lus brgya yongasu bstan pa dang / lus re re la yang byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor brgya yang dag par
67b8(phal chen): dbum par bya ba'i brtsod 'grus kyi rnam pa de lta bu rtsom mo// de yan chang byang chub sems dpa'i smod lam gyi byad par gyis rnam par 'phrul te/ de dag gi lus sam 'ong ngam/ rdzu 'phrul lam/ mig gam/ spyod yul las/ dbyangs pa/ 
68a1(phal chen): spyod pa 'am/ rgyan tam/ byin gyi brlabs sam/ mos pa 'am/ mngon par 'du byed pa dag kyang bskal pa brgya phrag du ma dang / bskal pa stong phrag du ma dang / bskal pa brgya stong phrag du ma dang / bskal pa bye
68a2(phal chen): ba khrag khrig brgya stong du mas kyab bgrang bar dka'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos sa'i don 'di nyid yang brtag par bya ba dang / bstan par bya ba'i phyir de'i tshe/ tshig su bcad pa 'di dag spras so// de dag dkar po'i chos bas
68a3(phal chen): dge ba phun ldan zhing / deng gshegs yong su bsnyen bkur snying rje byams ldad la/ dang brgya che dge sems pang tshul dag ldan pa/ rgyal ba'i ye shes don du rlangs chen sems kyang skyed/ rgyal ba chos rdzogs 'gro ba yongasu bsgru do
68a4(phal chen): du thams cad mkhyen pa sangs rgyas spongs spyod brtan mthu can/ brtse rab chen pos chos kyi 'khor lo bskod bya bas/ rgyal ba'i zhing spyod sems kyi dam pa rab tu skyed// 'gro bar rnam pa sna tshogs dus rnams
68a5(phal chen): bstan pa'i phyir// 'dren pa kun gyi yon tan thams cad 'dod tshol zhing / dus gsum skad cig gcig tu mi rtog shes byed pa'i// mkha'a'adra shin tu yangs pa'i sems dang ldang bar byed/ shes rab nga
68a6(phal chen): sngar snying rje sngon 'gro thabs ldan zhing // mos dang bsam pa rnam dag stobs kyis tshad med la/ chags med mngon gyur gzhan gyi dring la mi 'jog pa// bde gshegs rnams dang mnyam gyur sems kyi dam pa skyed// bde gshegs
68a7(phal chen): sras sems rin chen yang dag skyes 'phral du// byis pa'i spyod bral sangs rgyas rnams kyi spyod dang ldan// stobs bcu mnga' rigs kha na ma tho med par skyes// bde gshegs mnyam nyid rjes rtogs byang chub mchog tu nges/ 'di 'dra'i sem
68a8(phal chen): dang sa 'thob lhan cig mngon par skyes/ bsam pa mi g.yor yi rgyal po 'dra bar gnas// rab tu dga' zhing spro mang dang dang ldan pa ste// mos pa'i shugs yang rtag par sems kyi mchog dang ldan/ 'jug dang 'tshe ba med cing khro
68b1(phal chen): ba med pa ste// ngo tsha shes shing srid zhu drang ldan shin tu bsdams// 'gro ba yongasu bslab pa'i mtshungs med ye shes dran gyur cing // 'dod par bya ba'i gnas dang ldan gyur dga' ba spyad// sa thob gyur ma thag tu 'jigs pa lnga dang bral/

68b3(phal chen): yo par mang / nyin dang mtshan du dge ba'i phyogs la sten byed cing // sems can don du chos brtson 'dod skying phyir ma yin// dge ba'i chos thos bsam la mkhas shing gnas med spyod// thob sems sred bral byang chub sems la rtag

68b6(phal chen): nga'i do du spong las mngor bar bsgyud // dam chos yongasu gzung zhing drang srong drung 'gro dang / spyod pa mchog gi ngong du smod lam mngor bar smra// sems can yongasu srid bya sangs rgyas zhing spying ste/ de'i zhing bachog rgyal sras kun

71b3(phal chen): yid dang / snying rje chen po med pa dang / gzhan las thos pa'i spyi rje su 'brang bas/ shes rab kyi rnam par yongasu bsgoms ra/ nyan thos kyi theg pa yongasu sgrub po// de'i gong du gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa dang / rang mngon par 'tshang
71b4(phal chen): rgya ba dang / snying rje chen po dang / babs mkhas pa med bdang rjed cing 'dra la bar 'byung bzab par khong du chud pas yongasu smras pa/ rangs ngas rgyas kyi theg pa yong su spyad po// de'i gong du yangs shing chang med
71b5(phal chen): pa'i sems dang / snying brtse zhing snying rje ldan pa dang / thabs mal sa pas yang dag par bzung ba dang / smod lamo chen po shin tu btab pa dang / sems cad thams cad yongasu mi gtong ba dang / sa

71b7(phal chen): 'di dag 'di rnam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan par yongasu spangs pas stobs thob par 'gyur ba dang / mi 'jigs pa bzhi thob pa nas rnam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yongs su 'grub pa
71b8(phal chen): yang dag par sgrub bo// de lta bas na bdag gis dge ba bcu'i las mngon par bsgru du 'dra ba la rnam pa thams cad du yongasu spyang 'ang ngor bar bsgrub pa la brtson par bya'o/ zhes ras/ de 'di ltar yang dag par slob ste/ mi dge
72a1(phal chen): bcu'i las kyi lam 'di ngag bsten pa dang / bsgongs pa dang mang du byas pa'i shas che bas ni sems cad dmyal ba'i rgyur 'gyur ro// 'bring gi byol song gi skye gnas kyi rgyur 'gyur ro// tha mas ni gshin
72a2(phal chen): dza'i 'jig rten gyi rgyur 'gyur te/ de la srog gcod pas ni sems can dmyal bar khrid do// byol song gi skye gnas su khring ngo // gshing rje'i 'jig rten du khring ngo // denas ji ste mir skyes na yang rnam par spod pa gnyis mngon bar bya
72a3(phal chen): ba 'di lta ste/ me thung ba dang / nang yang ba'o// ma byin par len pas ni sems can dmyal bar khring ngo // byol song gi skye gnas su khring ngo // gshing rje'i 'jig rten du khring ngo // de nas ci ste mir skyes na yang rnam par smin pa gnyis mdze
72a4(phal chen): bar sgrub pa 'di lta ste/ longs spyod chung ba dang / thun mongs gi longs spyod du 'gyu ra ro// 'dod pas log par g.yem pas ni sems can dmyal bar khrid ngo // byol song gi skye gnas su khrid do// gshin rje'i
72a5(phal chen): 'jig rten du zing ngo // de nas ci ste mir skyes na yang rnam par smin pa gnyis mdo na bar bsgrub pa 'di lta ste/ ldong pa dang bcas pa'i chung ma dang / g.yog 'khor mi srun pa'o// brdzun du smra bas ni sems
72a6(phal chen): can dmyal bar khrid do// byol song gi skye gnas su khrid ngo do// gshin rje'i 'jig rten du khring ngo // de nas ci ste mir skyes ma yang rnam par smon pa gnyis mngon par sgrub pa 'di lta ste/ skud pa mang ba dang / gzhan gyis bslu ba'o//

73a1(phal chen): skyed cing de 'di snya du sems te/ kyem sems can 'di dag ni lha bangang la lung bdag ste/ blo gros mi mnyam zhing bsam pa mi mnyam pa log pa'i lam pibs por rgyu ba yin gyis/ de dag bdag gis bde
73a2(phal chen): ba'i lam yang dag par lta ba'i lam// de ba'adi nyid ji lta ba bzhin la rab tu dgod par bya'o// e ma'o sems can 'di dag ni mi mthun zhing rtsod pa dang / 'thab pa la zhugs pa rtag tu rgyun mi 'chang par khro ba dang / khong du 'dzin pas

76b1(phal chen): zags nang na rtag tu dgras gtse zhing // bdud kyi chom po'i nang gnas de dag bdag gis dgrol// nyon mongs rlabs kyis g.yengs shing chu bo bzhir nub pa// khams gsum sdug bsngal brgya yis yong su gdungs pa'i rnams// phung po'i gnas
76b2(phal chen): la rten cing bdag tu 'du shes pa// de dag sdug bsngal dgrol don bdag gis brtson par bya// sangs rgyas ye shes dam pa rmad byung phul spangs shing // 'byung ba yod bzhin dma' ba'i blo gros skyed byed pa// de dag de bzhin gshegs
76b3(phal chen): pa'i ye shes yangs dgod ces// rgyal ba'i ye shes don du brtson 'grus yangs pa rtsom// 'di gnas yon tan brgya bsngags drang srong chen po rnams// bde gshegs du ma mthong zhing mchod pa'ang rab tu byed// dge ba de dag bskal
76b4(phal chen): pa bye bar phyir zhing spong / gser gyi dam pa nag tshur nang du bcug pa bzhin// 'di gnas rgyal sras 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal por 'gyur// dge ba bcu la sems can rab tu dgod pa byed// dge tshogs gang yang rung ste spyo
76b5(phal chen): bar byed pa'i rnams// spobs bcu ldan zhing 'gro ba'i skyabs 'gyur don du stsogs / 'dod nga rgyal po'i srid kyang rnam par spangs byas shing // bstan pa 'i rnams ni bstan pa'i mchog la rab byung nas// brtsom
76b6(phal chen): 'grus ldan zhing ting 'dzin dam pa mchog kyang 'thob// sangs rgyas stong tshad skad cig gcig gis mthong bar byed// 'di 'dra'i tshul gyi bgrang bas gzhan yang gcig min pa// khyu mchog sa 'di gnas pa rab tu ston pa byed// de'i
76b7(phal chen): gong na ye shes smod lam mchog ldan pa// rnam par 'phrul pa rnam pa du mas sems can 'dul// de ltar sa mcho gnyis pa 'di // 'jig rten kun la phan 'dod pa'i// byang chub sems dpa'i mchog rnams la// bde bar ba
76b8(phal chen): pa'i sras kyis bstan// dri ma dang bral ba zhes bya ba ste// byang chub sems dpa'i sa gnyis pa'o// / rab pa ba'i dgra dang byang chub sems dpa'i spyod yul
77a1(phal chen): / bsam yas pa// sa mchog spyod pa de skad thos gyur nas// rgyal ba'i sras rnams rab tu dga' zhing sti stang du// me tog sprin char kun nas mngon par 'bebs// ri'i rgyal por bong ba legs so legs/ 
77a2(phal chen): sems can kun la snying brtse bsam pa yis// sa mchog dam pa'i spyod yul de 'dra dang // mkhas pa'i tshul khrims sdom pa khyod kyis bshang // yang dag de dngos ma nor gzhan med pa'i// byang chub sems dpa'i smod pa yid 'ong
77a3(phal chen): zhing sa sems can kun la phan dang bde bar rab sems pa// phul du 'od gsal khyod kyis bstan pa byas// da dung nga cung lnga dang mis mchod cing // chos kyi ye shes rigs par brjod mkhas pa// de dag spyod yul tshul
77a4(phal chen): ni ji bzhin du// sa yi ma pa gsum pa brjod par mdzod// drang srong chen po'i spying tshul spyod pa dang / bzod pa brtson 'grus zhi ba shes rab thangs// byams pa'i mchog dang snying rje lam gyi rnams/ 
77a5(phal chen): rgyal sras spyod pa rnab spang bsun mdzod cig/ rdo rje'i snying po 'jigs me ngal// rnam grol zla bas yang smras pa// gsum la yang dag 'phar 'gyur ba'i// bsam pa babs pas bshad ba mdzod/ 
77a6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying pos smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sa gnyis pa la bsams pa shin tu spangs pa ni/ sa gsum pa yongs su gnon te/ de sems
77a7(phal chen): kyi bsam pa yid la bya ba bcus yongasu gnod to// bcu gang zher 'di lta ste/ dag pa'i sems kyi bsam pa yid la bya ba dang / mi g.yo ba'i sems kyi bsam pa yid la bya ba dang / skyo ba'i sebs kyi bsam pa yid la bya ba
77a8(phal chen): dang / 'dod chags dang bral ba'i sems kyi bsam pa yid la bya ba dang / phyir mi ldog pa'i sems kyi bsam pa yid la bya ba dang / brtan pa'i sems kyi bsam pa yid la bya ba dang / sbyangs pa'i sems kyi bsam pa yid la
77b1(phal chen): bya ba dang / rlom sems kyi bsam pa yid la bya ba dang // rlabs po che'i sems kyi bsam pa yid la bya ba dang / bdag nyid che ba'i sems kyi bsam pa yid la bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag byang chub sems dpa' byang
77b2(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i sa gsum pa la gnas pa ni 'du byed kyi rnam pa thams cad la mi rtag par yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu rtog go// sdug bsngal ba dang / bdag med pa dang / mi sdug pa dang / yid brtan du mi rung ba dang
77b3(phal chen): rnam par 'jigs pa dang / ring du mi gnas pa dang / skad cig tu 'byung zhing 'gag pa dang / mi zab cing mi skye mi 'gag pa dang / sngon gyi mtha' kun nas ma byung ba dang / phyi ma'i mtha' 'pho ba med pa dang
77b4(phal chen): ra lngar byung ba mi gnas pa rab tu rtog go// de 'du byed kyi rnam pade lta bu la rab tu rtog pa'i tshe/ mngon par 'jig pa dang / mya nga can smre sngags 'don pa cad/ 'khrug pa can/ yid du 'ong
77b5(phal chen): dang yid du mi 'ong bas rnam par bcings pa sdug bsngal dang ying mi bde bamang ba/ bsngags pa med ba las byung ba/ 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug gi me rab tu 'bar ba
77b6(phal chen): nang du mas rnam par skyed pa/ sgyu ma'i rang bzhin lta bur mthong nas/ de de bas kyang 'du byed thams cad las sems gyen du spyod cing de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes la rab tu gtong ste/ des de bzhin gshegs pa'i
77b7(phal chen): ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab pa'ang rjes su mthong ste/ batshungs pa med pa dang / gzhal du med pa dang / rnyed par dka' ba dang / ma 'dres pa dang / gnod pa med pa dang / 'khrug pa med pa dang / mi 'jigs pa'i grong
77b8(phal chen): rdul du 'gro ba dang / phyir mi ldog pa dang / 'gro ba mang po yongasu slob pa yang yang dag par rje su mthong ngo // des de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes de ltar tshad med pa mthong ste/ 'du byed kyi rnam pa de ltar sdug bsngal ma
78a1(phal chen): bos gtses par mthong nas/ sems can thams cad la de bas kyang shas cher sems kyi bsam pa bcu che bar gzhog sde bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lnga sde/ dgor ba dang / skyabs med pa dang / rten med pa'i se
78a2(phal chen): kyi bsam pa dang / rtag tu phongs pa'i sems kyi bsam pa dang / 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang / gti mug gi me kun nas 'bar ba'i sems kyi bsam pa dang / srid pa'i btson ras bzung ba'i sems kyi bsam pa dang / rtag tu rgyun
78a3(phal chen): mi 'chang bar nyon mongs pa'i thibs pos bsgribs pa'i sems kyi bsam pa dang / brtag pa'i mthu med pa'i sems kyi bsam pa dang / dge ba'i chos la mos la mos pa med pa'i sems kyi bsam pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos
78a4(phal chen): thams cad las shin tu grol ba'i sems kyi bsam pa dang / 'khor ba'i rgyud kyi rjesu 'bab pa'i sems kyi bsam pa dang / thar pa'i lam gyis spangs pa'i sems kyi bsam pa dang / sems kyi bsam
78a5(phal chen): pa 'di bcu nye bar gzhog go// des de lngar sems can gyi khams gtse ba ma nga po can mthong ras brtson 'grus 'di ltar rtsom ste/ sem sa can 'di dag ni bdag gis bsrung par bya ba yongasu dgrol
78a6(phal chen): bar bya ba/ yongasu spyang bar bya ba/ shin tu gdor par bya ba/ rab tu dgod par bya ba/ shin du brtan par bya ba/ yong su tshim par bya ba/ gnas su phyir bar bya ba/ rnam par gdul bar bya ba/ yongasu mya ngaran las 'da' bar
78a7(phal chen): bya ba yin no// zhes nas/ de de ltar 'du byed kyi rnam pa thams cad las skyo ba'i rjes su song zhing sems can thams cad la rab tu lta ba'i rjesu song ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye
78a8(phal chen): shes kyi rjesu song zhing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes la rab tu rten pas sems can thams cad yongasu bskyab par bya ba la brtson pa de 'di ltar yongasu rtog ste/ rgyu dang gzhi ngang tshul dang thabs gang zhig gis 'di lta bur
78b1(phal chen): sdug bsngal dang / nye ba'i nyon mongs par ltung ba'i sems can 'di dag mngon par gdon par nus/ rgyu dang gzhi ngang tshul dang thabs gang zhig gis ni shim tu bde ba'i mya ngan las 'das par dgong par nus spam nas// de la byang chub seMs
78b2(phal chen): dpa' 'di snyam du sems te bsgribs pa med pa'i ye shes rnam par thar pa'i gnas ma gtogs par gzhan gyis mi nus so// bsgribs pa med pa'i yis rnam par thar pa'i gnas de yang chos thams cad yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin khong du
78b3(phal chen): chung ba ma gtogs par gzhan gyis thob par mi nus so// chos thams cad yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du khong du chud ba yang / rgyu ba med cing skye ba med pa la spyod pa'i shes rab ma gtogs par gzhan gyis khong du chud bar mi nus so// 
78b4(phal chen): shes rab kyi snang ba de yang bsam gtan la mkhas shing rtogs pa'i blos rab tu rtog pa med par gzhan gyis thob par mi rung ngo // bsam gtan la mkhas shing rtogs pa'i blos rab tu rtogs pa de yang thos pas mkhas pa
78b5(phal chen): med par mi 'byung ngo zhes/ de de ltar shin tu brtags pa'i shes pa dang ldan bas/ de bas kyang shas mer dam pa'i chos tshol ba la mngon bar brtson par gnas te/ nyin mtshan du chos mnyan pa don du
78b6(phal chen): gnyer ba yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos btsal ba'i don du chos la mos shing ngoms mi shes la rgyun mi 'chad pa yin/ chos la dga' zhing spro ba dang chos la rab tu 'jug pa yin/ chos la gzhol zhing chos la 'bab pa dang
78b7(phal chen): chos la bab pa yin/ chos la chen cing chos la skyabs tshol ba dang / chos la mthu tshol ba yin/ chos dang gnyer ba'i chos la mngon par brtson pa yin te de de ltar chos tshol ba la mngon par brtson pas rim po che'i rnam pa'ang
78b8(phal chen): dbyig gi rnam pa 'am/ nor dang 'bru'i mdzod dang / bang ba gang yang rung ste yongasu mi gtong ba de lta bu gang yang med do// chos smra ba'i gang zag de 'ba' shig la dga' ba'i 'du shes su gyur pa las par/ de dag gzhan
79a1(phal chen): la cung zad kyang dga' ba'i 'du shes mi skyed do// de ni chos kyi don du phyi rol gyi dngos po nye bar gzung ba yongasu mi gdong ba de gang yang med do// nang gi dngos po yongs su mi gtang bar bya ba de lta bu'ang cung zad
79a2(phal chen): kyang med do// gang 'di dag 'di lta ste/ g.yog 'khor yongasu btang ba 'am/ rgyal srid yongasu gtang ba 'am/ longs spyod yongasu btang ba 'am/ nor dang 'bru dang nor bu dang / gser gyi mdzod dang / bang pa yongasu btang ba dang / 
79a3(phal chen): dang glang po dang shing rta dang / gzhon pa yongasu btang ba 'am/ rin po che'i rgyan dang / lhab lbub yongasu gtang ba dang / chung ma dang bu dang / bu mo yongasu gtang ba 'am/ mgo dang rga lag dang / yang lag gi dam pa yongasu gtang ba'am/ 
79a4(phal chen): lus thams cad yong su gtang bar bya ba yang rung ste/ de dag thams cad chos kyi don tu mong su mi gtong ba gang yang med do// bla ma la bsnyen bkur dang / rim gror bya ba gang yang rung ste nyams su mi len pa gang yang
79a5(phal chen): rung ste nyams su mi len pa gang yang med do// nga rgyal dang lhag pa'i nga rgyal yongasu gtang bas nga rgyal med pa la spyad pa gang yang rung ste/ nyam sa su mi len pa gang yang med do// lus kyi gnod pa gang yang

113b8(phal chen): bar shes pa dang / ye shes chen ba spu'i ting nge 'dzin sa yongasu spyong bar byed pa/ brgya stong phrag bcu tshang ba la snyoms par 'jug go// de thabs dang shes rab kyis yongs su sbyangs pa'i ting nge 'dzin de dag rab tu thob
114a1(phal chen): pa dang / snying rje dang snying brtse ba'i mthus nyan thos kyi sa las 'das pa yin/ rang sangs rgyas kyi sa las 'das pa yin/ shes rab dang ye shes kyis rnam par dpyad pa'i sa mngon sum du gyur pa yin

118b3(phal chen): ba dag pas mchod// gser spra ma de nyid rin chen mang pos spras pa bzhin// 'di la gnas pa'i mkhas pa'i shes rab mchog gi 'od // sred pa'i chu rnams ji ltar nyi bzhin yongasu sems/ 
118b4(phal chen): sa mchog 'di la gnas pa dbang spya rgyal por 'gyur/ ye shes ngam pa'i 'bras bu sngon la mthu yod mkhas// 'dod na brtson 'grus dam pa'i stobs dang ldan gyur pa/ sangs
118b5(phal chen): rgyas bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong tshang pa dag/ phyogs rma/ mas kum tu shin tu mnyam par bzhag pas mthong / yan chad smon lam yo matan mchog can tshad kyang med
118b6(phal chen): 'dis mis mchog bdun pa ste/ rang rgyal dbang la spyod pa dang // 'jig rten kun gyis shes par dka'// thabs dang shes rab spyong ba'o// ring du song ba zhes bya ba ste/ 
118b7(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i sa bdun pa'o// / bam po lnga bcu pa/ mkhas pa'i spyod pade 'dra ngam pa thos mos// lha'i tshogs dang lnga'i dbang po
118b8(phal chen): dga'// byang chub sems dpa' 'gro phan brtson pa mang po/ bde bar gshegs dang rgyal sras rnams mchod byed/ phreng ba rgyal mtsham pa ngan yid 'ong // spos dang phye ma rin chen na ba
119a1(phal chen): rgyan pa// dbyig gis spras pa'i gdugs rag drag khrig dum/ phreng ba'i sprin gyi ngam pa'i char yang 'angon 'bengs// lha'i bu mos yid du 'ong ba'i sgra dbyangs// du ra'i sil snyar par gyi
119a2(phal chen): mchog dang ldan byas// de gshegs dang rgyal sras mchod pa'i don du// thub pa'i yon tan rmad du byung ba brjod byed// thams cad gzigs pa rkang gnyis khyu mchog gtso bo// sangs rgyas spyod yul 'gro la
119a3(phal chen): phan phyir stor mdzad// dbyangs sprin yid du 'ong ba rab tu 'byung ba yi ni// rdza dang sil snyan sna tshogs rnams la 'di thung // skra'i rtsel bde gshegs brgya phrag spong steng // 'gag 'ga' khrag khrig bye ba'i rdul
119a4(phal chen): bas ngangang // sim chog ngas pa mnyam pa med pa ga na/ kyu mchag 'angs ni rdul bral tshas rnams sngon mdzadabacig rgya la byas byas dam pa'i mings// rlung bani dus rgya
119a5(phal chen): mtsho chen kun nas// khor yug bye ba de bzhin ri rab thams cang // so so'i tshul dang ldan par kun kyang snang gyur// sgra 'i rtse mo de la 'gro rgyud drug po// yi gas byol song mi
119a6(phal chen): sems dmyal lnga dang // gnod sbyin srin po klu dang lnga min mang ngo po// sno tshogs las kyi yul la kun kyang spyod byed// rdul bral kun gyi ming gi spyod yul kun tu// 'khor lo dam pa'i mchog kyang
119a7(phal chen): 'khor gyur// 'gro ba'i 'du shes sems dang de bzhin spyod pa// bde gshegs gsung gi dam pa kun kyang bstan byas// sems can lus la bde gshegs zhing mang sna tshogs// zhing la sems can rmad
119a8(phal chen): steng lus kyang de bzhin// lha dang mi'i lam rgyud de bzhin sna tshogs// mkhyen nas bde bar gshegs pa chos rnams kun ston// shin tu yangs pa'i zhing la 'du shes phral gyur/ rdul gyi mtshan ma ngag la 'du shes
119b1(phal chen): yangs gyur// de la sogs pa bde bar gshegs pa'i rdzu 'phrul// 'jig rten kun gyis brjod kyang zad par mi 'gyur// che ba nyid dbyangs de skad du// snyan pa'i dbyangs su grag gyur nas// 'khor rnams rab tu dga'
119b2(phal chen): zhing zhi// gsung ba'i mchog la lha zhing gnas// 'khor rnams zhi bar shes gyur nas/ rnam grol zla bas yang smras pa// sa brgyad pa yi rnam pa dang // de lnga 'jug pa bstan par mdzod// byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i
119b3(phal chen): snying pos smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub sems dpa'i sa bdun pa la rnam par dbye ba shin tu byas pa// thabs dang shes rab kyis lam shin tu spangs pa/ cho
119b4(phal chen): shin tu bsags pa/ smon lam chen po shin tu btab pa'i slob sa dang shugs can de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis shin tu brla bas pa rang gi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i spobs dang shugs thob pa/ de bzhin
119b5(phal chen): gshegs pa'i spobs dang / mi 'jigs pa dang / sangs rgya sa kyi chos ma 'dres pa yid la bya ba dang ldan pa/ bsam pa dang / lhag pa'i bsam pas yongasu spyang ba'i sems dang ldan pa
119b6(phal chen): bsod nams dang ye shes kyi spobs kyis mngon par 'phags pa/ snying rje dang snying brtse ba chen pos sems can gyi khams thams cad yongasu mi gtong ba'i spor ba dang ldan pa/ ye shes kyi lam tshang med pa'i
119b7(phal chen): rjesu song ba/ de chos thams cad thog ma nas ma byung ba nyid la yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du 'jug// ma skyes pa dang / mtshan nyid med pa dang / skye ba med pa dang / 'jig pa med pa dang / thug pa med pa dang / 
119b8(phal chen): mi rgyu ba dang / mi ldog pa dang / dngos po med pa'i rang bzhin dang / thog ma dang tha ma dang / dpung mnyam pa nyid dang / de bzhin nyid kyis rnam par mi rtog pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la'ang yang
120a1(phal chen): dag pa ji lta ba bzhir du 'jug ste/ des rnam pa thams cad du sems dang yid dang / rnam par shes pa'i rnam par rtog pa dang / 'du shes dang bral zhing thogs pa med pa la ma mkha' dang 'dra
120a2(phal chen): zhing namakha'i rang bzhin du khong du chud pas mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob ces bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag de la de lta bu'i bzod pa dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa mi g.yo ba thob
120a3(phal chen): ma thag tu byang chub sems dpa'i gnas zab mo shes par dka' ba tha mi dad pa mtshan ma thams cad dang bral ba/ 'du shes kyi bgegs thams cad las phyir log pa tshad med pa nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams
120a4(phal chen): cad kyis mi 'phrogs pa dben pa thams cad mngon du gyur pas/ shin tu thob pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag 'di lta ste dper na/ dge slong rdzu 'phrul dang ldan pa/ sems thams cad la dbang thob pa/ 
120a5(phal chen): mthar gyis 'gog pa'i bar du mnyam par bzhag pa'i rgyu ba dang / sems pa dang / g.yo ba'i rnam par rtog pa dang / 'du shes thams cad dang bral ba yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag
120a6(phal chen): de bzhin byang chub sems dpa' yang / byang chub sems dpa'i sa brgyad pa mi g.yo ba 'di thob ma thag tu ched du bya ba thams cad dang bral te lhun gyis grub pa'i chos nyid thob cing lus dang ngag dang / sems kyi rtsom
120a7(phal chen): ba thams cad dang bral te/ shin tu dper ba'i chos nyid la gnas pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag 'di lta ste dper na/ mi la la zhig gnyid kyis log pa'i rmi lam du bdag chu klung chen pos khyer snyam byed
120a8(phal chen): la/ de de nas ci phyin du 'bad cing rtsol ba chen po rtsom rtsom pa las de 'bad cing rtsol ba chen po de nyid kyis sang bar gyur na/ de sang ma thag tu 'bad cing rtsol ba thams cad dang bral bar 'gyur ro// kye rgyal ba
120b1(phal chen): sras ngag de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang nyon mongs pa'i chu klung chen po bzhir sems can mang po dong bar shes nas 'bad cing rtsol ba yongasu rtsom mo// de brtson 'grus chen po dang ldan pas byang chub sems dpa'i sa mi
120b2(phal chen): g.yo ba 'di thob ma thag tu ched tu bya ba thams cad dang bral ba yin te/ de'i gnyis po rgyu ba 'am mtshan ma rgyu ba dag kyang thams cad kyi thams cad du mi snang bar 'gyur ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag 'di lnga ste dper na tshangs pa'i
120b3(phal chen): 'jig rten du skyes shing gnas pa ni/ 'dod pa la spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa yong su mi rgyu ba yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin du byang chub sems de po'i sa mi g.yo ba la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yang sems dang
120b4(phal chen): yid dang rnam par shes pa'i yongasu rgyu ba rnams thams cad kyi thams cad tu yong su mi rgyu ba yin te/ de sangs rgyas la yong su rgyu ba 'am/ byang chub la yongasu rgyu ba 'am/ byang chub sems da
120b5(phal chen): la yongasu rgyu ba 'am/ rang sangs rgyas la yong su rgyu ba'am/ nyan thos la yongasu rgyu ba'am/ mya ngan las 'das pa la yod su rtsu ba 'am/ dgra bcom pa la yongasu sgyub 'am/ phyir mi 'ong ba
120b6(phal chen): yongasu rgyu ba 'am/ lan cig phyir 'ong ba la yong su rgyu ba 'am/ rgyun tu zhugs pa la yongasu rgyu ba yang yong su mi rgyun 'jig rten pa'i yongasu rgyu ba lnga ci smos/ kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag de ltar mi bayo ba'i sa la
120b7(phal chen): gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sngon gyi spod lam gyi spobs dang shugs la gnas bde'i chos kyi spong rgyud de la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyis nye bar bsgrubapa
120b8(phal chen): mthang de de la 'di sad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu legs so legs so// sangs rgyas kyi chos rjes su rdzogs par bya ba la 'di mi ngomangs pa'i bzod ba yang yin na/ 'on kyang rigs kyi rgya
121a1(phal chen): stobs bcu dang / mi 'jigs pa bzhi dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos phun sum tshogs pa de khyod la med kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi chos phung sum tshogs pa de dag yongasasu btsal ba'i phyir btsun
121a2(phal chen): 'grus rtsoms shig/ bzod pa'i sgo 'di nyid kyang ma gtang shig/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ khyod kyis de ltar zhi ba'i rnam par thar pa thob kyang byis pa so so'i skye bo 'di dag zhi ba ma yin/ rab tu zhi ba ma yin te/ nyon mongs
121a3(phal chen): pa sna tshogs yongasu rgyu bar gyur na/ de ltar rnam par rtog pa sna tshogs kyis yongasu mnar ba la soms/ ji ltar yang rigs kyi bu khyod kyi sngon gyi smon lam sems can gyi don yongasu 'grub par bya bar btab pa dang / 
121a4(phal chen): ye shes kyi spo bsam gyis mi khyab pa dram par gyis shig/ 'di ltar yang rigs kyi bu 'di ni chos rnams kyi chos nyid de/ de bzhin gsheg/ sa ba rnams byung yang rung ma byung yang rung / chos kyi dbyings dang chos
121a5(phal chen): kyi gnas nyid 'di ni de bzhin du 'dug pa ste/ 'dis ni de bzhin gan/ gas pa rnams nyi tshe brjod par bya ba ma yin te/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas rnams kyang rnam par mi rtog pa'i chos nyid 'di 'thong
121a6(phal chen): go// rigs kyi bu khyod ded kyi lus tshad med pa dang / ye shes tshar med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing tshad med pa dang / ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa tshang meng pa dang / 'od kyi dkyil 'khor tshad med pa dang / dbyangs kyi yan lag
121a7(phal chen): rnam par dag pa tshad med pa la ltos/ khyod kyis kyang de bzhin du mngon par bsgrub par bya dgos so// 'di ltar rigs kyi bu gang de ltar chos thams cad la rnam par mi rtog pa de ni khyod kyi snang ba gcig pur zad de/ rigs
121a8(phal chen): kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi chos snang ba ni 'di 'dra ste/ yongasu mtha' yas par song la yongasu mtha' yas par bsgruslus pa ste/ de snyed kyi bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gis kyang bgrang bar dgas/ de dag / 
121b1(phal chen): par bya ba'i phyir mngon par bsla ba skyed cig 'di ltar ying rigs kyi bu phyogs bcu'i zhing tshad med pa dang / sems cad tshad med pa dang / chos rnam par bye ba tshang med pa la khros te/ de dag thams cad mnor bar bgrang bar
121b2(phal chen): gyis shig/ ces te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de ltar de lta bu'i ye shes dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' la/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa'i sgo de dag la sogs pa gang gis byang chub

121b6(phal chen): bsgrub pa'i las gang gis skad cig thang gcig tu mngon par bsgrubs pas kyang thog ma sems bskyed pa phyin chad sa bdun la zhugs shing rje su song ba'i yongasu rtsom pa'i bar snga ma de dag gis brgya'i char yang nye bar mi
121b7(phal chen): 'gro/ stong gi cha dang / khrag khrig gi cha dang / brag khrig brgya'i cha dang / khrag khrig stong gi cha // khrag khrig brgya phrag stong gi cha dang / bye ba khrag khrig brgya phrag spong gi char yang nye bar mi 'gro'o// grangs dang

122a1(phal chen): lus gcig gis mngon par bsgrub pas spyod pa mngon par bsgrub par gyur gyi 'di la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni lus rnam par phye ba tshad med pas/ byang chub sems
122a2(phal chen): dpa'i spyod pa'i mthu yong su sdud de dbyangs mngon par bsgrub pa tshad med pa dang / ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa tshad med pa dang / skye ba mngon par bsgrub pa tshad med pa dang / zhing yongasu spyong pa tshad med pa dang / sems can

122a4(phal chen): dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor tshad med pa rnam par phye ba dang / tshad med pa'i rjesu song ba'i lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las kyis byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyi mthu mi sprul ba'i tshul gyis yang

122a6(phal chen): ma thag tu rlung gi dkyil 'khor gyis bsu bas ched du bskyod mi dgos pa yin/ des rgya mtsho chen po la nyin gcig gis ci tshong ba de ni sdom du bskyod cing 'gro bas lo brgyar yang de ltar tshad med par phyin par mi nus so//

122b1(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag de la byang chub sems dpa'i sa brgyad pa'ing thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' mi thabs mkhas pa'i ye shes kyis bsgrub pa lhun gyis grub pa la shin tu zhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i blos thams

123a1(phal chen): bye ba yang rab tu shes so// de shin tu phra ba'i rdul phra ba nyid kyang shin tu shes so// shin tu phra ba'i rdul yangs pa yang rab tu shes so// shing tu phra ba'i rdul tshad med pa yang rab tu sheso//

123a3(phal chen): ngag kyang rab tu shes so// me'i khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba de dag kyang rab tu shes so// rlung gi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba de dag kyang rab tu shes so// rin po che rnam par phye ba ji snyed pa yod pa dang / rin po che'i rdul shin tu phra ba

123a8(phal chen): shes so// gzugs kyi khams 'jig pa yang rab tu shes so// gzugs med pa'i khams 'jig pa yang rab tu shes so// 'dod pa'i khams 'du ba yang rab tu shes so// gzugs kyi khams 'du ba yang rab tu sheso//

123b2(phal chen): par phye ba'ang rab tu shes so// gzugs kyi khams dang / gzugs med pa'i khams chung ba'ang rab tu shes so// che ba'ang rab tu shes so// tshad med pa'ang rab tu shes so// rnam par phye ba yang rab tu shes so// de khams
123b3(phal chen): gsum rnam par spyad pa'i ye shes khong du chud pa mngon par bsgrubs pa'i ye shes kyi snang ba dang ldan la/ sems can gyi lus rab tu dbye ba la mkhas shing zhing gi lhun rnam par dbye ba'i ye shes la mkhas pas skye ba'i skye mched
123b4(phal chen): thams cad mngon par bsgrub pa la blo shin tu gdong ste/ de ni sems can yongasu smon par bya ba'i phyir/ sems can rnams kyi skye ba dang / yongasu grub pa ci 'dra ba de lta bur/ rang gi lus byin gyis rlob / 
123b5(phal chen): nga sdang gsum gyi spong chen po'i 'jig chen gyi khams rgyas par ba/ nga zhing sems can gyi mos pa ji lta ba de bzhin du rang gi lus ji lta ba de bzhin du rang gi lus mig yor lta bu'i ye shes kyi rje su 'dra
123b6(phal chen): bas skye bar bya ba'i phyir mngon par sgrub ste/ stong gsum gyi spong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams gnyis sam gsum 'am/ bzhi 'am/ lnga 'am/ bcu 'am/ nyi shu 'am/ sum cu'am/ bzhi bcu 'am/ lnga bcu ga
123b7(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar dag rgyas par bkang ste/ sems can gyi mos pa ji lta ba de bzhin du rang gi lus mig yor lta bu'i ye shes kyi rtasu 'brang bas skye bar bya ba'i phyir mngon par bsgrub bo// de de lta bu'i ye
123b8(phal chen): shes dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig nas kyang mi g.yo la/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa dag gi de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dag tu yang snang bar phyin pa yin/ ngo sems can rnams kyi
124a1(phal chen): lus rnams kyi phye ba dang mos pa dang / bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du zhing de dang de dag dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de dang de dag tu de ltar de ltar rang gi lus ston te/ de dge sbyong gi 'khor
124a2(phal chen): gyi dkyil 'khor du dge sbyong gi kha dog dang gzugs ston to// bram ze'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du bram ze'i kha dog dang gzugs ston to// rgyal rigs kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du rgyal rigs kyi kha dog dang gzugs so
124a3(phal chen): // rje'u rigs kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du rje'u rigs kyi kha dog dang gzugs sngon to// khyim bdag gi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du khyim bdag gi kha dog dang gzugs sdong ngo // rgyal po chen po bzhi'i rigs kyi 'thor
124a4(phal chen): gyi dkyil 'khor du rgyal po chen po bzhi'i rigs kyi kha dog dang gzugs ston to// sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'a khor du sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i kha dog dang gzugs ston to// de bzhin du
124a5(phal chen): tshe ma'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dang / dga' ldan gyi 'khor rgya 'akyil 'khor dang / 'phrul dga'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khorarang gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dang / tshangs
124a6(phal chen): pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor nas 'og min gyi dkyil 'khor gyi bar du de lta de lta bu'i kha dog dang gzugs ston to// de nyan thos kyis 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la nyan thos kyi lus dang / kha dog dang gzugs storan to// 
124a7(phal chen): rang sangs rgyas kyi 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la rang sangs rgyas kyi lus dang kha dog dang gzugs ston to// byang chub sems dpas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i lus dang / kha dog dang ba
124a8(phal chen): sngon to// de bzhin gshegs pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dang kha dog dang / sku gzugs ston to// kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag de ltar sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa ji snyed pa de dag gi
124b1(phal chen): sems can rnams kyi mos pa rab tu mang ba de dag thams cad du rang gi 'alus de lta de ltar rnam par phye ba yongasu ston to// de lus kyi rnam par rtog pa dang / 'du shes thams cad dang rnam par bral ba ste/ lus mnyam pa nyid
124b2(phal chen): thob pas sems can gyi lus rab tu shes so// zhing gi lus dang las kyi rnam par smin pa'i lus dang / nyan thos kyi lus dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi lus dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lus dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dang
124b3(phal chen): ye shes kyi lus dang / chos kyi lus dang / namakha'i lus kyang rab tu shes so// nges sems can rnams kyi sems dang bsam pa mngon par bsgrub pa yongasu shes pas 'dod na/ sems can gyi lus mamakha'i lus su byin
124b4(phal chen): gyis rlob bo// de bzhin du ning gi lus dang / las rnam par smin pa'i lus dang / nyan thos kyi lus dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi lus dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lus dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dang / ye shes

124b6(phal chen): gyis rlob bo// de bzhin du zhing gi lus dang / las rnam par smin pa'i lus dang / nyan thos kyi lus dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi lus dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lus dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dang / ye

124b8(phal chen): 'dod pa de dang de'i lus su lus de dang de dag byin gyis rlob bo// de sems can gyi lus gyi lus rnams kyi las kyi lus kyang rab tu shes so// rnam par smin pa'i lus dang / nyon mongs pa'i lus dang / gzugs kyi lus dang / 
125a1(phal chen): gzugs med pa'i lus kyang rab tu shes so// ming gi lus rnams kyis chung ba'i rang bzhin yang rab tu shes so// che ba dang tshad med che ba dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par dag pa
125a2(phal chen): dang snrel zhi dang / spyi'u tshugs dang / bzhi mnyam par yang dag par 'jug pa dang / phyogs kyi dra ba rnam par dbye ba yang rab tu shes so// las rnam par smin pa'i lus rnam par phye ba'i brda' yang rab tu shes so// de bzhin du
125a3(phal chen): nyan thos kyi lus rnam par phye ba'i brda' dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi lus rnam par phye ba'i brda' dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lus rnam par phye ba'i brda' yang rab tu shes so// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rnams kyi mngon par 'tsha
125a4(phal chen): rgya ba'i lus kyang rab tu shes so// smon lam gyi lus dang / sbrul pa'i lus dang / byin gyi rlabs kyi lus dang / gzugs dang mtshan dang / dpe byang bzang ba'i rgyar gyi lus dang / tha~Md kyi lus dang / yid
125a5(phal chen): kyi rang bzhin gyi lus dang / bsod nams kyi lus dang / ye shes kyi lus dang / chos kyi lus kyang rab tu shes so// ye shes kyi lus rnams kyi shin tu rnam par dpyad pa nyid kyang rab tu shes so// 
125a6(phal chen): yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du brtags pa yang rab tu shes so// 'bras bu'i sbyor bas yang dag par bzung ba dang / 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa rnam par phye ba dang / theg pa gsum rnam par dgod pa dang / thun
125a7(phal chen): mongs dang / thun mongs ma yin pa dang / 'byung ba dang / mi 'byung ba dang / slob pa dang / mi slob pa yang rab tu shes so// chos kyi lus rnams kyi mnyam pa nyid kyang rab tu shes so// 'khrug pa med pa rab tu shes so// 
125a8(phal chen): gnas dang brda' dang / kun rdzob rnam par dgod pa dang / sems can dang sems can ma yin pa'i chos rnam par dgod pa dang / sangs rgyas dang / chos dang / 'phags pa'i dge 'dun rnam par dbong ba yang rab tu shes so// 
125b1(phal chen): rnam pa'i lus rnams kyi tshad med pa nyid kyang rab tu shes so// thams cad kyi rjesu song ba dang / lus med pa dang / nor ba med cing / mtha' yas pa dang / gzugs mang po mngon zhing gsal bar byed pa yang rab tu shes so// nges
125b2(phal chen): lus kyi ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa de lta bu rab tu thob pas bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par tshe byin gyis brlabs pa'i phyir tshe dbang rab tu 'thob po// ting nge 'dzin shin tu rtogs pa'i ye shes la 'jug par bya ba'i
125b3(phal chen): phyir/ sems kyi dbang rab tu 'thob bo// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyan du mas rab tu brgyan cing shin tu klubs pa'i byin gyis brlabs yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir yo byad kyi dbang rab tu 'thob bo// las kyi rnam pa
125b4(phal chen): smin pa'i byin gyi brlabs dus bzhin du ma nor bar bsum pa'i phyir las kyi dbang rab tu 'thob 'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du skye ba yongasasu bstan pa'i phyir/ skye ba'i dbang rab tu 'thob bo// sangs rgyas
125b5(phal chen): kyi zhing dang / dus gang du ci dga' bar mngon par 'tshang rgya ba la nga dag par bstan pa'i phyir smon lam gyi stobs rab tu 'thob bo// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sangs rgyas kyis rab tu
125b6(phal chen): gang ba yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir mos pa'i dbang rab tu 'thob bo// sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du rdzu 'phrul dang / rnam par 'phrul pa yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir rdzu 'phrul gyi spobs rab tu 'thob bo// de bzhin ga
125b7(phal chen): pa'i stobs dang / mi 'jigs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa dang / mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang / mngon par 'tshang rgya ba yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir ye shes kyi dbang rab tu 'thob bo// mtha' dang dbus
125b8(phal chen): med pa'i chos kyi ste snang ba yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir chos kyi dbang rab tu 'thob bo// de byang chub sems dpa'i dbang bcu po 'di dag thob ma thag nas bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i ye shes dang ldan pa yin/ tshad med pa'i
126a1(phal chen): ye shes dang ldan pa yin/ yangs pa'i ye shes dang ldan pa yin/ mi 'phrogs pa'i ye shes dang ldan pa yin/ des de lta bu rjesu song zhing de lta bu'i ye shes dang ldan pas lus kyi las kha na ma
126a2(phal chen): ba shin tu med pa yang dag par rgyu zhing 'byung ba yin/ ngag gi las kha na ma tho ba shin tu med pa yang dag par rgyu zhing 'byung ba yin/ yid kyi las kha na ma tho ba shin tu med cing ye shes sngon du 'gro ba ye shes rje su 'brang ba shes rab
126a3(phal chen): kyi pha rol tu phyin pas dbang sgyu ba/ snying rje chen po sngon du 'gro ba'i thabs mkhas pas shin tu rnam par phye ba smon lab gyis shin tu mngon par bsgrubs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs pa/ sems can gyi

126a6(phal chen): sa mi g.yo ba 'di thob pas nyon mongs pa'i rgyu ba thams cad dang bral ba'i phyir bsam pa'i spobs shin tu brtan pa yin/ lam dang mi 'bral ba'i phyir lhag pa'i bsam pa shis tu brtan pa yin/ sems can gyi don yongasu ma
126a7(phal chen): gtong ba'i phyir/ snying rje chen po'i stobs shin tu brtan pa yin/ 'gro ba thams cad yongs su skyob pa'i phyir/ byams pa chen po'i spobs shin tu brtan pa yin/ nyams pa med pa'i chos dang ldan pa'i phyir gzungs kyi spobs shin
126a8(phal chen): tu brtan pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad ga tu dbye ba'i bye brag la mkhas pa'i phyir spobros pa'i bus shin tu brtan pa yin/ 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' yas par spyod pa'i rnam pa la mkhas pas mngon par shes pa'i stobs
126b1(phal chen): / shin tu brtan pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa'i bya ba thams cad yongasu mi gtong bas smon lam gyi spobs shin tu brtan pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yang dag par bsgru pa'i phyir pha rol tu phyin pa'i spobs shin tu brtan pa yin/ 
126b2(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes rnam pa thams cad du mngon du gyur pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs kyi stobs shin tu brten pa yin te/ de de lta bu'i stobs kyi shugs dang ldan pas bya ba thams cad kyang yang dag par ston/ 
126b3(phal chen): bya ba thams cad la kha na ma tho ba'ang med pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi sa brgyad pa ste/ mi 'phrogs pa'i phyir mi g.yo ba zhes bya'o// ye shes mi zlog pa'i phyir mi 'gyur ba zhes bya'o// 
126b4(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad kyis shes par dka' bas na thob par dka' ba'i sa zhes bya'o// kha na ma tho ba med pa'i phyir gzhon nu'i sa zhes bya'o// bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin dbang sgyu bas skye ba'i sa zhes bya'o// gzod bya ba

126b7(phal chen): lta bu'i ye shes mngon par bsgrubs pa dang ldan zhing / sangs rgyas kyi rigs kyi rjesu song ba/ sangs rgyas kyi yon tan gyis shin tu gsal bar gyur pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod lam dang spyod pa dang / tshul gyi rjes
126b8(phal chen): du song ba/ sangs rgyas kyi yul la mngon du gyur pa de mi rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs pa yin/ brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi mgon pos rab tu bsu ba yin/ lag na
127a1(phal chen): rdo rje'i dag par rjesu 'brang ba yin/ ting nge na gyi bas yong sum btang ba yin/ lus rnam par phye ba tshad med pa mngon par grub pa yin/ lus kyi spyod pa'i spobs thams cad ldan pa yin

127a7(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i sa mi g.yo ba thob pa yin zhes bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag de la byang chub sems dpa'i sa mi g.yo ba thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i ni ting nge 'dzin gyi stobs kyis mngon par bsgrubs pas rtag

127b1(phal chen): khams 'angam klas pa re re dag du yang / sangs rgyas dum dang / sangs rgyas brgya phrag dus sa sangs rgyas stong phrag du ma dang / sangs rgyas brgya stong phrag du ma dang / sangs rgyas bye ba brgya stong brag du ma dang / sangs rgyas

127b8(phal chen): gser gyi sa le sbram de nyid mgar ba mkhas pa des yongasu zin par gyur nas/ 'dzam+bu'i gling gi bdag po'i mgul lam/ mgo la btags na sems cad 'dzam+bu'i gling ba thams cad kyi rgyan gyi rnam pa
128a1(phal chen): kun gyis mi thung mi 'phrogs pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i sa mi g.yo ba 'di la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thang

128a3(phal chen): sems can rnams kyi nyon mongs pa'i mun pa rab tu sel to// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di lta ste dper na/ spong la dbang ba'i tshangs pa ni stong gi 'jig rten gyi khams byams pas bkang zhing 'od kyi snang bar byed do// kye rgyal ba'i sras
128a4(phal chen): ngag de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i sa mi g.yo ba 'di la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yang sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya stong phrag pa cu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi bar gyi 'jig rten gyi khams snang bas
128a5(phal chen): rgyas par bkang zhing sems can rnams kyi nyon mongs pa'i yongasu gdung ba mthar gyis zhi bar byed do// lus kyang shin tu tshim par byed do// de'i pha rol tu phyin pa bcu las smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i
128a6(phal chen): shas che ba yin te/ lhag ma rnams kyang ci tshul ci nus su yang dag par mi sgrub pa ma yin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa mi g.yo ba zhes bya ba ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa brgyad pa mdor bstan pa'o// 
128a7(phal chen): rgya cher ni bskal ba mu med pas bstan pa'i mthar thug par shes par bya'o// de la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni phal cher srong gi bdag po tshangs pa chen por 'gyur te/ gzhan la zil gyis gnon cing / gzhan gyis mi
128a8(phal chen): non pa dang / don mthong zhing dbang thob par 'gyur te/ sems can rnams la nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ston pa la mkhas shing mthu yod pa yin/ 'jig rten gyi khams rnam
128b1(phal chen): par phye ba yongasu dris pas mi 'phrogs pa yin/ de sbyin pa 'am/ ngag snyan pa 'am/ don bsgrub pa 'am/ don 'thun pas dge ba'i rtsa ba gang ci rtsom yang rung ste/ de thams cad ji ltar na sems can thams cad kyi mchog tu 'gyur
128b2(phal chen): gtso bor 'gyur/ thu bor 'gyur/ phul du 'gyur/ dam par 'gyur/ bla na med par 'gyur/ 'dren par 'gyur/ yong su 'dren par 'gyur ba nas thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la rten pa'i bar du 'gyur snyam ste/ sangs rgyas
128b3(phal chen): yid la bya ba dang / chos yid la bya ba dang / dge 'dun yid la bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yid la bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sa yid la bya ba dang / pha rol tu phyin pa yid la bya ba dang / stobs yid la bya ba dang
128b4(phal chen): mi 'jigs pa yid la bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa yid la bya ba nas/ rnam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi bar du yid la bya ba dang mi 'bral ba yin te/ 
128b5(phal chen): de 'dod na skad cig yud tsam thang gcig tu ting nge 'dzin stong gsum brgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyeng rab tu 'thob cing de dag la snyoms par 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas stong gsum brgya
128b6(phal chen): stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed mthong ba dang / de dag gi byin gyi brlab sa kyang yang dag par shes pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams stong gsum brgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed spyod pa dang / sangs rgyas
128b7(phal chen): kyi zhing stong gsum brgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du 'gro ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams stong gsum brgya stong phrag rdul shin tu phra ba snyed snang bar bya ba dang / sems can stong gsum brgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul
128b8(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed longasu smin par bya ba dang / bskal pa stong gsum brgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du gnas par bya ba dang / sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' bskal pa stong gsum brgya stong phrag
129a1(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed la rab tu 'jug pa dang / chos kyi sgo stong gsum brgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rnam par 'byed pa dang / lus stong gsum brgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba
129a2(phal chen): snyed yongasu bstan pa dang / lus re re la yang byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor stong gsum brgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yang dag par bstan par bya ba'i phyir/ brtson 'grus kyi rnam pa de lta bu rtsom mo// de yan chad
129a3(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i smon lam gyi mthu can rnams/ smon lam gyi khyad par gyis rnam par 'phrul te/ de dag gi lus sam/ 'ong ngam/ rdzu 'phrul lam/ mig gam/ spyod yul lam/ dbyangs sam/ spyod pa 'am/ rgyan tam/ 
129a4(phal chen): byin gyi rlabs sam/ mos pa 'am/ mngon par 'du byed pa dag kyang bskal pa du ma dang / bskal pa brgya phrag du ma dang / bskal pa spong phrag du ma dang / bskal pa brgya stong phrag du ma'i bar gyis kyang bgrang ba
129a5(phal chen): dka'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos sa'i don/ 'di nyid yang brtag par bya ba dang / bstan par bya ba'i phyir de'i tshe/ tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smra so// de dag sa bdud shes rab
129a6(phal chen): thabs kyis lam spangs shing // shin tu tshogs bsags smon lam chen po rab btab pa// mau'i dam pas byin brlabs dge ba'i rtsa ldan zhing // ye shes mngon 'dod mkhas pa brgyad pa yongasu gnon// bsod nam
129a7(phal chen): ye shes nye bas gas snying rje byams ldan zhing // tshad med sems kyi rjes song mkhas dang 'dra ba'i blo// drang srong chen po chos thos rtogs pa'i stobs ldan pa// mi skye'i bzod pa phra zhing zhi ba rab tu 'thob// snga nas ma skyes
129a8(phal chen): mi skye mtshan nyid med pa dang // ma byung 'jig pa med cing rgyu ba med pa dang // dngos po skye 'jig med pa'i de nyid rtog med pa// yid dang sems kyi rgyu ba med cing namakha' 'dra// de dag 'di 'dra'i bzong ldan spros pa med gyur
129b1(phal chen): pa'i/ dam khas bzab spyong zhi ba'i gnas rab thob pa yin// dgra bcom rang rgyal 'gro ba kun gyi shes par dka'// mtshan ma sna tshogs 'dzin pa'i 'du shes rnam par bsal// de ltar gnas pa'i ying dang sems dang rtog
129b2(phal chen): ba med// dge slong 'gog dang ldan ltar rnam par mi rtog thob// rmi lam chus khyer gnyid sad bzhin du rtsom dang bral/ tshangs pa'i gnas kyi 'dod pa ji bzhin gnyid kyang med/ sngon gyi byin gyis bde gshegs
129b3(phal chen): yang dag sprul pa mdzad// 'dzin bde gshegs dbang bsung bzod pa dam bste/ nged kyi ye shes spobs yangs sangs rgyas chos kyi rnams// de dag khyod la med kyis de la brtson 'grus brtsoms// ci phan khyod kyi nyon
129b4(phal chen): mongs 'bar ba kun zhi yang // 'jig rten nyon mongs mes tshig de dag mi lta bar// sems can phan phyir spyad pa'i sngon gyi smon lam soms// 'gro ba mthar rgyur ye shes ngom zhugs shes par gyis/ 
129b5(phal chen): chos nyid de bzhin nyid 'di mi rtog rtag tu 'dug/ sa 'di rgyal ba nyan thos rang rgyal kun gyi ste// 'dis ni 'jig rten ngag tu stobs bcu mi brjod do// gzhan du ye shes yangs bdus
129b6(phal chen): gsum tshad kyis brjod// de ltar de la mtshungs med lha dang mis mchod pa/ ye shes sgo mo rnam mang nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad// rgyal ba'i chos sgrub pha rol mtha' las gzhug mdzad pa/ de la sngon gyi byang chub
129b7(phal chen): spyod pas char mi 'gro// khyu mchog de dag ye shes sa mchog 'di thob nas// phyogs rnams kun tu skad cig gcig gis rgyas 'gengs pa// ye shes zhugs dang ldan zhing mngon shes mchog thob pas// 
129b8(phal chen): mtsho cher phyin gru chen rlung gis bkur ba bzhin// ched du bskyod sems bral zhing ye shes las la gnas// zhing rnams 'byung zhing gnas pa rnam par dpyod pa byed// khams rnams bzhi po kha dog tha dad yangs pa
130a1(phal chen): dang // phra zhing che dang rnam par phye la yang dag 'jug/ stong gsum shin tu rdul phra kun la 'jug byed de// khams bzhi 'gro ba'i lus rnams rnam par phye ba dang // rgyud drug rin chen rnam par
130a2(phal chen): phye ba'i rdul phran rnams// rnam par phye zhing ye shes yul gyis ma lus 'brang // ye shes rnam bsgoms yid ldan lus rnams thams cad du/ la 'gro ba'i don phyir rang gi lus rnams gzung bar byed/ stong gsum thams
130a3(phal chen): cad sna tshogs gzugs kyis khyab byas shing // 'jig rten mtha' yas ngag tu sna tshogs lus kyang sngon// bar snang mkha' la nyi zla rlung gis rgyu 'gro yang // so so'i dkyil 'khor gzugs brnyan chu dkyil rab tu snang // 
130a4(phal chen): bzhin mi g.yo'i chos la ye shes dam pas rgyu// bsam dag 'gro ba rnams la mkhas pa'i gzugs brnyan snang // 'gro ba'i bsam ba bzhin du lus kyi rna phye ba// mi dang lha'i 'khor rnams kun tu ston pabyed
130a5(phal chen): nyan thos rang rgyal bde gshegs sras kyi lus rnams dang / bde bar gshegs sku yan lag brgyan pa rab tu ston// sems can zhing dang de bzhin las kyi rnam smin lus// 'phags lus sna tsho
130a6(phal chen): de bzhin chos dang ye shes lus// namakha'i lus dang mnyam pa nyid du khyu mchog ldan// rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs 'gro ba tshim par bya phyir ston// dbang bcu dri ma med pa'i ye shes dpyod pa thob// ye shes sbyong dang las
130a7(phal chen): rnams snying rje 'thun pa'ang thob// las rnams ji snyed rgyal ba'i chos rnams yongasu bsgrub// sdom pa gsum la gnas shing mi g.yo ri rab bzhin// rgyal sras rnams kyi spobs bcu bskyod par mi nus pa// de dag
130a8(phal chen): kun nas bdud rnams kun gyi yong mi zlogs// sangs rgyas byin brlabs brgya byin tshangs pas phyag kyang bya// lag na rdo rje'i dpung rnams rtag tu phyi bzhin 'brang / sa phyogs 'di la gnas pa'i yon tan mtha'
130b1(phal chen): yas te// de dag bskal ba khrag khrig spong gis zang mi nus// de dag sangs rgyas bye ba bsnyen bkur yang byed pas// rgyal po'i mgo la 'dug pa'i rgya bzhin shin tu gsal// sa phyogs 'di gnas byang chub sems
130b2(phal chen): dpa' shes ldan pa// spong gi bdag po tshangs chen yon tan mang por 'gyur// theg pa gsum sngon yongasu mi 'khrugs mi 'phrogs te// 'od bzangs byams pa'i bsam pas 'gro ba'i nyon mongs sel// skad cig
130b3(phal chen): gcig tu stong phrag bcu'i zhing rnams kyi// rdul khams ji snyed de snyed ting 'dzin ldan pa thog pa phyogs bcu'i sems can gtso bo de snyed mang po mthong // yan chad smon lam mchog gi rgyan can gcig min no// 
130b4(phal chen): 'di mdor bsdus rgyal sras kyi// sa brgyad shin tu bstan ba ste// rgya chen bskal pa bye bar yang // thams cad mthar phyin/ mi nus so// byang chub sems dpa'i sa brgyang ba sde mi g.yo ba zhes
130b5(phal chen): bya ba'o// bam po lnga bcar gcig pa/ sa yi ngas pa 'di bshad tshe// nga bzhin gshegs pa'i byin brlabs kyis// tshang
130b6(phal chen): med bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i// bye ba'i zhing rnams g.yos par 'gyur// thams cad gzigs pa'i sku las kyang // 'od zer yid du 'ong ba bkye// des ni zhing rnams snang bar byas// sems can rnams kyang bde
130b7(phal chen): bar gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' stong snyed kyang // bar snang gnas la 'khor gyur te// lnga rdzas ldog pa'i mchod pa yis/ gsungs pa'i mchog la mchod pa byed/ lnga yi rgyal po dbang phyug dang / 
130b8(phal chen): yang sgyu rlams kyang dga' bar gyur// mchong ba rnam pasna tshogs kyis/ yom tan rgya mtsho mtshang ba byed// de nas lnga mi bu ma song // dpa' zhing dbang po bder gyur pas/ sbrur legs snyar pa
131a1(phal chen): klu yi dbyangs// ston pa mchod pa'i don du len// rol mo'i sgra dbyangs de dag las// drang srong chen po'i byin brlabs kyis// 'di 'dra'i sgra dbyangs stong snyed du// snyan pa'i dbyangs su grags
131a2(phal chen): par gyur// 'i dul rab zhi dri ma thams cad med gyur cing // sa yi mchog dang ldan pas spyod pa legs spyod pa// phyogs bcur 'gro la phan par spyod pa'i khyu mchog rnams// mkha' dbyings 'dra ba'i yid kyis rgyal ba'i spyod
131a3(phal chen): ba ston// mi'i gnas dang lha'i gnas dang klu gnas su// phyogs bcur bsod nams stobs kyis rgyan rnams mang po byung // de las yang du rgyal sras ye shes lam mos pa// rgyal ba'i yon tan bsngags pa rgya chen
131a4(phal chen): rab tu ston// zhing gcig ma g.yos rdul ming zhing rnams thams cad du// 'gro la phan byed zla ba lta bu'i 'od ldan pa// thams cad dbya sa su 'du shes sems zhi yid rab kyis// so so skang bzhin sgra
131a5(phal chen): snang brgya yang rnam par brjod// sems can gang rnams blo nanas/ mas ming dmar gyur ba// de la mkhas pa khyu mchog nyan thos spyod pa sngod// sems cad gang rnams sems no rang rgyal theg
131a6(phal chen): brtsom pa// de la rdul med rang rgyal theg pa'i ye shes ston// sems can gang rnams phan sems snying rje rtse yid can// de la de dag rgyal sras spyod pa'i mchog kyang ston// sems can gang rnams blo mchog dam pa'i
131a7(phal chen): yid mos pa// de la mkhas pa tshad med sangs rgyas sku ston to// ji ltar sgyu mkhan 'gro ba rnams la smra ston pa// lus mang bye ba sna tshogs de dag dngos po med// de bzhin rgyal sras mkhas pa ye shes smra mkhas pa// spyod pa
131a8(phal chen): sngon kyang de dag dngos po med// 'di 'dra'i sgra skad brgya stong du// snyan pa'i dbyangs su brjod byas nas// lha yi bu mo mi smra bar// zhi la mos pas rgyal ba lta// 'khor rnams rnam par dang bas na// bde gshegs sras
131b1(phal chen): la yang smras pa// dam chos spyod pa'i spyod pa rnams// brgyad pa'i gong du yang gsungs shig/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa'/ byang chub sems dpa'i

131b3(phal chen): ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsang ba'i rjesu 'jug par bya ba la 'jug pa dang / ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i che ba nyid rnam par dbye ba dang / gzungs dang ting nge 'dzin rab tu dbye ba yong su spyang ba dang / mngon
